National People's Livelihood Postal Service

Unanimous Suspension of Business Today for Major Petition 147

To Petition the Municipal Government, Party Headquarters, and Garrison Headquarters in the Morning

Take the Night Train to Beijing to Appeal to Chairman Chiang and the Fifth Plenary Session

丨Gather Representatives from Suzhou, Changzhou, Wuxi, and Zhenjiang Along the Way to Beijing丨

Five hundred branches of the People's Livelihood Postal Service from twelve provinces across the country will unanimously suspend business today (13th) and dispatch seven general representatives, including Yin Yuantong, to petition the five agencies of the Municipal Government, Municipal Party Headquarters, Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Municipal Public Security Bureau at 9:00 a.m., requesting that the termination not be enforced until the central government has decided on a plan to handle the livelihoods of more than 100,000 employees of the People's Livelihood Postal Service. They will also take the night train to Beijing at 11:00 p.m. to join more than 100 representatives from twelve provinces gathered in Beijing to appeal to Chairman Chiang and the party and government agencies such as the various yuan and departments. A reporter from the East China News Agency has investigated and reported the details as follows:

Petition in the Morning 148

Since the Ministry of Communications ordered all People's Livelihood Postal Services in the country to be terminated uniformly within this year, the colleagues of the People's Livelihood Postal Service in twelve provinces across the country, with the livelihoods of more than 100,000 people about to be cut off and the aftermath difficult to maintain, have successively dispatched representatives to Shanghai to gather and discuss the aftermath. After having petitioned in Beijing once, and there being no result, they have repeatedly convened representative conferences in Shanghai, deciding to suspend business for one day today across the country to hold a major petition, and dispatching the general representatives of the Shanghai People's Livelihood Postal Service, Hua Yunjin, Shao Yuantong, Wang Dashi, Zhuang Gengtang, Qiu **Sheng, Ren Shiting, and Pan Wentian, to petition the five agencies of the Municipal Government, Municipal Social Affairs Bureau in the central area of the city at 9:00 a.m. today, and the Municipal Party Headquarters, Songhu Garrison Headquarters on Longhua Road, and Municipal Public Security Bureau in the city at 11:00 a.m., requesting that the termination not be enforced until the central government has decided on a plan to handle the aftermath, in order to maintain the livelihoods of more than 100,000 employees of the People's Livelihood Postal Service.

Petition to Suspend 149

A document from the entire employees of the National People's Livelihood Postal Service presented to the various yuan, departments, committees, bureaus, and Chairman Chiang reads: "The People's Livelihood Postal Service is currently requesting a postponement of the limited-time termination disposition. However, as the deadline is approaching, we first appeal for a suspension of the reported implementation before the central government has made a decision on a plan, in order to show consideration and stabilize society. The People's Livelihood Postal Service has a long history of establishment. Before the establishment of the postal service in our country, the people relied on it for transmitting letters and transporting goods. Commerce flourished because of it, and society was stable because of it. The government protected it, as seen in its proclamations. After the postal service was established, it initially felt inexperienced in performing its duties, and the People's Livelihood Postal Service guided and helped it, especially with its merits. Therefore, after the promulgation of the Postal Law, the Ministry of Communications still formulated registration and licensing methods to maintain it. In recent times, the General Post Office has been ordered by the Ministry to investigate the situation of private postal services, but it does not investigate the current situation and immediately presents a memorial to crack down on them. The Ministry is unaware and strictly orders the termination, with an urgent deadline that cannot be delayed. Although the postal service should be state-owned, which is a common practice in countries around the world, the timing of promoting unification should take into account the national conditions. In today's situation in China, the People's Livelihood Postal Service still has a value in existence. It is true that the transmission in large cities does not rely on the People's Livelihood Postal Service, but in remote rural areas, post offices have not yet been universally established, and it is difficult to implement the crackdown, resulting in a loss of convenience. Furthermore, in terms of the livelihoods of the employees, once the business is terminated, they will have nothing to rely on, and they will be forced into hunger and cold. The old and weak will turn to ditches, and the young and strong will take risks, which is not a blessing for society. While the authorities have the determination to unify the postal service, they should also consider the People's Livelihood Postal Service's aftermath solution while actively improving it, in order to provide relief. However, they are making decisive dispositions, and society is affected, and the employees are especially deeply affected. Therefore, representatives of colleagues from various ports across the country held a joint conference at the Shanghai Postal Service Association, resolving to petition the Fifth Plenary Session and the central government agencies based on the above reasons, and dispatching the presenters as the general representatives of the National People's Livelihood Postal Service to request your Ministry, Government, and Bureau to review and approve, and to temporarily suspend the Ministry of Communications' execution of the consultation to assist in ordering the People's Livelihood Postal Service to terminate at the end of the 22nd year, until the central government has a solution for the aftermath and this matter has been decided, in order to show consideration. We are extremely eager to await orders. Respectfully presented to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, Municipal Government, Public Security Bureau, Social Affairs Bureau, and Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the general representatives of the National People's Livelihood Postal Service, Hua Yunjin, Yin Yuantong, Wang Dashi, Zhuang Gengtang, Yin **Zhensheng, Ren Shiting, and Pan Wentian."

To Beijing Tonight 150

In addition to dispatching seven representatives to petition the five party and road agencies in this city, the industry has also scheduled to take the night express train to Beijing at 11:00 p.m. tonight to join more than 100 representatives of the People's Livelihood Postal Service from twelve provinces who have already gathered in Beijing to petition the five agencies of the Fifth Plenary Session, the Executive Yuan, the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Ministry of Communications, and to appeal to Chairman Chiang, who is in Beijing. It is also learned that representatives of the People's Livelihood Postal Service from Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Danyang, Zhenjiang, and other places along the Jinghu Road will also go to Beijing on this train.

Aftermath Difficulties 151

According to Yin Yuantong, chairman of the People's Livelihood Postal Service Association, the difficulties of our industry cannot be fully expressed in one sentence. The People's Livelihood Postal Service was founded in the seventh year of Guangxu, earlier than the post office, and has been around for more than 100 years. There are more than 500 People's Livelihood Postal Service companies in twelve provinces across the country, with more than 100,000 employees. Of these employees, 60% to 70% are laborers who have always been hardworking and can endure hardships, running hundreds of miles on rural roads to maintain their livelihoods. Now, the authorities of the Ministry of Communications suddenly ordered the General Post Office to crack down on them, and ordered them to terminate at the end of the year, so the lives of these more than 100,000 People's Livelihood Postal Service employees and their families will be cut off, and they will sit and wait to die. Therefore, representatives from various places have been dispatched to Shanghai to gather and discuss solutions. It has been decided that tomorrow (i.e., today) will be a day of full suspension of business, first petitioning the party and government agencies in this city, and then entering Beijing that night to petition the Fifth Plenary Session and the various yuan and departments, and also to appeal to Chairman Chiang in Beijing, asking him to consider the difficulties of the merchants and pity the lives of more than 100,000 employees and hundreds of thousands of employee family members, and grant an extension of the termination period so that they can gradually change industries during this period, so that hundreds of thousands of people can temporarily maintain their livelihoods. As for the pros and cons of the People's Livelihood Postal Service and the postal service, the People's Livelihood Postal Service can deliver bulky packages that cannot be mailed by the post office, such as large luggage and oily objects, so people in society all consider it convenient. Therefore, once terminated, not only will the people be inconvenienced, but hundreds of thousands of people will also have difficulty maintaining their lives.

Armored Vehicles, Machine Guns, Cavalry, and Artillery All Deployed

Full Mobilization 153

Participants include a total of thirty teams of members from China, Britain, the United States, Japan, Russia, Germany, Scotland, the Philippines, Norway, Denmark, Portugal, and the Jewish community. Fully Armed 154

Exercise Locations 155

The exercise locations are divided into three locations: the West District, the North District (including the extraterritorial roads), and the North Sichuan Road area. (1) The West District is for the infantry team, on the extraterritorial roads east of the Route de Triumphe, and the cavalry team is west of the Route de Triumphe; (2) The North District is for the infantry team, at the intersection of the North Henan Road, North Zhejiang Road, North Xizang Road, and the Boundary Road with the Chinese boundary; (3) The North Sichuan Road, within the Public Concession, and the Linping Road area. In order to avoid misunderstandings among citizens, the Bureau will issue announcements at the time, and will also ask the neighboring authorities to post announcements in the areas concerned.

Cable Request to Maintain Soybean Oil Import Tax 158

Soybean oil in our country has always been a major food item. In the past, the number of products produced in the northeastern provinces was relatively prosperous, and tens of millions of dans were transported to Shanghai every year, causing the oil market in Shanghai to be manipulated for a long time, and the oil mill business gradually declined. After September 18, the government of our country set the import tax on goods transported from the northeast to China at 15% of the value of industrial and commercial products and 30% of the value of food oils, in order to maintain domestic industry and commerce. The oil mills in Shanghai were fortunate to sprout after the rain, and the future was promising. However, recently, it was suddenly heard that someone used the excuse of opposition to secretly submit to the government a request to cancel the previous order. The oil mill colleagues were all surprised and abnormal. Yesterday, the industry association convened a general meeting and immediately resolved to cable the government. The text is as follows: "To President Wang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, and Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, regarding the food soybean oil formerly transported from the northeast to Shanghai, the original tax rate was 15% of the value. Recently, it has been largely changed to 30% of the value in order to eliminate dumping and manipulation in the northeast and maintain our country's industry and commerce. The future of the industry is deeply reliant on this. However, recently, it has been heard that someone used the excuse of opposition to secretly submit a large amount to the ** requesting the cancellation of the previous order. It is found that soybean oil has always been a major food item in our country, and it is only used by industry and commerce. If the previous order is cancelled again, it will inevitably still allow the northeast to dump, manipulate, and destroy domestic products without anything left. We are frightened and earnestly submit our words, respectfully requesting your review, and we will await orders, Zhu Jingan, Chairman of the Shanghai Vegetable Oil Mill Industry Association, bows sincerely."

This member must be able to understand the situation in Shanghai in external affairs work within a considerable period of time, and then order him to preside over the traffic affairs. At the same time, a lower-level policeman will be selected as his assistant to prepare to take over external affairs.

The opinion of the Police Chief is that the person managing traffic must be a member who has come from ** police affairs. If a member is selected from the current personnel of the department, he can be sent to Europe to practice for a few months, and can obtain considerable knowledge, and is more suitable than a person hired from outside who is difficult to understand the local situation for a while. The opinion of the Director of Works is that the term "traffic engineer" only refers to a traffic commissioner with sufficient technical knowledge of traffic management. The personnel of the Works Department also have considerable knowledge of this. The Directors of the Works and Police Departments feel that the Works Department and the Police Traffic Section should have more close cooperation.

Ningbo Road Police Interference in Marriage Disputes 161

Ningbo Fellow-Countrymen Association: Negotiations with the Bureau of Public Works Director-General

Wang Yaoqing, a native of Zhenhai, reported that his wife had been seduced and had absconded, cohabitating with a policeman. The Ningbo Fellow-Countrymen Association dispatched personnel to escort her back to her husband, Wang Yaoqing. However, Wang's wife, née Li, was suddenly summoned and released by the Ningbo Road Police Station. The Ningbo Fellow-Countrymen Association believes that this action by the police station hinders the association's work and, on the previous day, sent a letter to the Bureau of Public Works Director-General, Mr. Zhong Si, and Co-Director Mr. He Zhongliu, making the following requests. The original letter is transcribed below:

"Respectfully informing you, our association is organized and established by Ningbo natives residing in Shanghai in the second year of Xuantong (1910). It is registered with the Chinese government as a legitimate civil organization. Our mission, in addition to handling charitable and public welfare undertakings, is to provide amicable mediation for various disputes among fellow countrymen, including those related to marriage and debt. Our history is long, and our reputation is well-established. There is no need for further elaboration from our association.

On the eighth of this month, our association received a report from our fellow townsman, Wang Yaoqing, stating that his wife, Li Guisu, had absconded with belongings to the upper floor of the Chai and Coal store at the Yong'an Lane entrance of Caojiadu, Robert Road, and was cohabitating with Police Officer No. 3333 of the 6th District Public Security Bureau. He was unable to bring her back and requested assistance. After confirming the marriage contract, our association sent our member, Dong Xinqin, accompanied by the aggrieved Wang Yaoqing, with a letter requesting assistance from Inspector Gu Wentao of the district's Public Security Bureau. Inspector Gu dispatched police assistance to escort Li Guisu back. Due to estrangement between the couple, our association was providing amicable reconciliation to achieve harmony.

Unexpectedly, at noon on the same day, the Ningbo Road Police Station accepted the false accusation of Li Guisu's mother, née Li Xu, and, without investigating the details, immediately sent detectives led by Zhang Yuanjing to the association. With a threatening manner, they took the parties involved, Wang Yaoqing and Li Guisu, away. Subsequently, they summoned our staff members, Dong Xinqin and Lin Zitong. After questioning revealed it was a marital dispute, the police station decided not to handle the case and arbitrarily released the runaway wife, Li Guisu, whom our association and the Public Security Bureau had escorted back. They also did not thoroughly investigate Li Xu, who had fabricated the false accusation.

The police station's handling of this case seems to lack due recognition of our association's position and clearly hinders our work. After deliberation by our association members, we unanimously assert:

(1) We request your bureau to investigate and reprimand the personnel responsible for handling this case.

(2) We request assurance that similar incidents will not occur again in the future.

Therefore, we briefly narrate the circumstances and request your esteemed Director-General to review and handle the matter and provide a reply."

Foot-and-Mouth Disease Outbreak Among Shanghai Cattle 162

Health Bureau Taking Preventative Measures

Beef Supply to Be Short in the Short Term

Foot-and-mouth disease has been discovered among cattle in Shanghai. This disease is an acute infectious disease of cloven-hoofed animals, characterized by vesicular rashes on the skin and mucous membranes, especially in the mouth and between the hooves. It is caused by a bacterium, and contact with secretions of the mucous membrane easily leads to infection. Once the toxin enters the bloodstream, it invades the deeper mucous membranes. If not prevented early, it can spread widely, significantly impacting both animal husbandry and the economy and potentially infecting humans.

It is reported that the outbreak was discovered early, and the Health Bureau, together with the Epidemic Prevention Institute and the Bureau of Public Works Health Department, is taking preventative measures, hoping to eradicate it soon.

According to news from the Bureau of Public Works Intelligence Office, at yesterday's (12th) Bureau of Public Works Board meeting, the Director-General presented a report stating that cattle transported to Shanghai from the interior have recently been found to have foot-and-mouth disease. The Bureau is cooperating with other government offices to eliminate this pestilence. However, the beef supply in Shanghai is bound to be short in the next two to three weeks.

Recently, veterinary officers from the Ministry of Industry, the Municipal Government, the French Concession, and the International Settlement held a meeting. They jointly confirmed that foot-and-mouth disease had broken out. However, the nature of the disease seems mild. It is generally found in cattle transported from northern Jiangsu and Anhui or is transmitted in transit. The medical officers decided to request the relevant government offices to prohibit the import of cattle from these areas. The authorities are making every effort to restore the meat supply to normal as soon as possible.

Exhibition Purpose 164

The exhibition is divided into two types: trademark exhibition and sample exhibition. Regardless of whether the products are machine-made or handmade, national products are the principle. Pingliang Road, Inside the New Port

Female Cadaver With Knife Wounds Discovered 178

Back of Neck and Throat Punctured

Appears To Have Been Moved and Dumped After Death

In the water inside the New Port at the side of an empty ground behind the Gongdi Spinning Factory at the bottom of Yangshupu, near the intersection of Pingliang Road, a female cadaver with knife wounds was discovered on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Someone caught a glimpse of it and reported it to the Yinxianggang Police Station, which telephoned the river police. The police station immediately dispatched Chinese Detective Shen Changshan, Liang Shenqing, and Western Detective Macdonald (transliteration) to inspect the scene. They found that the short-haired female cadaver was about 30 years old. She had a gold tooth on the left side of her mouth. She was wearing a red striped foreign cloth short shirt, a green boned white flannel undershirt, black maoge lined pants, striped flower flannel lined shoes, and a blue maoge unlined outer pants with a yuan-colored satin trim. She was wearing pink gauze socks and black wool high-topped cotton shoes. Next to the cadaver on the shore was a black camel hair qipao, with a blue foreign cloth qipao overcoat. A large hole was cut into the back of the cadaver's neck with a sharp blade before death. There were also two knife wounds on the left and right sides of the throat, and the trachea was severed, which was a very tragic sight. It was clearly a murder case where the body was moved and dumped here, so there was no water in the cadaver's abdomen.

The detectives then carefully investigated the surrounding area and found blood stains about 450 feet away from the cadaver, near the seventh lamp pole on Jungong Road. There was a hole of about three to four inches in the ground, in which vomited food was found. There was also fresh blood about 300 feet away from the hole. According to Chief Zhang Shixun of the police station, a large pair of scissors used for the crime was found near the bloodstain at the lamp pole. The blade of the scissors was covered in blood. There was also a white foreign-style green wooden comb inlaid with silver stars and a white handkerchief stained with blood.

The above three items were handed over by the detectives to Shen Changshan of the river police and taken back to the police station. After reporting the situation to the chief, the female cadaver was taken by boat to the Jinshapu beach in Nanshi and temporarily placed there. The chief prepared a letter together with the murder weapon, the comb, and the handkerchief, and ordered Detective Shen Changshan to submit them to the local court for an inquest.

Judge Wu Deying opened the court and summoned him for questioning. Detective Shen explained the situation and presented the murder weapon to the court. After the question officer examined it, he ordered to submit it for further review, then led Inspector Yi Zhiming to the scene, examined and concluded that the female cadaver had her throat cut with scissors before her death, causing her death. After completing the coroner's report, the officer ordered an examination and decided to put the body in a coffin while waiting to arrest the murderer to punish him.

Zhang Zhongyu's Son, Manager of the Siyi Silk Factory, Was Kidnapped

Used the Delivery of Red Eggs as a Pretext to Threaten With Guns 179

Kidnapped Zhang's Son Into a Car and Never Returned

Zhang Zhongyu, a native of Sheng County, Zhejiang, is 36 years old. He lives at No. 10, Lane 423 (i.e., Sencheng Lane) at the intersection of Kunming Road and Dalian Road in the Public Concession. His wife, née Tong, has two sons and two daughters. The eldest son, Geyang, is four years old, and the second son, Xiaoyang, is one year old. The eldest daughter, Puzi, is ten years old, and the second daughter, Xiaopu, is seven years old. Zhang has been in the silk business for many years, painstakingly managing it and making some progress. He and his friends jointly invested in the Siyi and Pingwei silk weaving factories in Qingfuli on Zhoujiazui Road and Huaxingfang on Baoding Road. Zhang was appointed as the manager of the two factories, unexpectedly attracting the attention of bandits.

Yesterday afternoon, a little after one o'clock, Zhang had gone out to discuss business matters and had not yet returned home. Three bandits suddenly came to his residence and knocked on the back door of Zhang's house. Zhang's wife was washing dishes in the kitchen at the time, and his eldest son, Geyang, was also nearby. When they heard someone knocking, they went to open the door and saw that one of the three men was carrying a small basket containing ten red eggs, and another man was holding a red invitation card. They asked to speak to Mrs. Zhang and claimed that someone had asked them to deliver the red eggs to Mr. Zhang. Mrs. Tong immediately replied that he had gone out and had not returned. The bandits then asked Mrs. Tong, "Are you Mrs. Zhang?" Mrs. Tong hesitated because the men looked suspicious. The bandits then went into the kitchen, took out a pistol, and threatened her. Mrs. Tong was shocked and quickly ran into the front hall. However, the bandits did not chase her, but exited through the back door, snatched her eldest son, Geyang, out of the lane, jumped into a car parked at the entrance of the lane, and sped away. By the time Mrs. Zhang realized what had happened and chased after them, they had already disappeared.

She immediately reported to the police station in charge, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to conduct a search and asked in detail about the clothing and appearance of the bandits. It was reported that one of the three bandits was wearing a black long robe, a small cap, and was about 40 years old. One was wearing a leather short jacket and was about 30 years old, and one was wearing a light gray long robe and was about 30 years old. All spoke with a Shaoxing accent and seemed very familiar with Zhang's family situation. The police are currently conducting a widespread search and arrest.

Li Xiaozhen and Yi Shizhu Were Both Raped

He also had young female performers Li Xiaozhen (13 years old, from Hangzhou, the younger sister of his concubine Yi Meimei, who came to Shanghai in August this year), Yi Shizhu (19 years old, from Hangzhou, Yi's cousin), Zhang Qincai (13 years old, from Shanghai), Chen Meiying (13 years old, from Hangzhou), Chen Fengying (16 years old, from Hangzhou), Yang Lindi (12 years old, from Pinghu), Chen Xiaofang (16 years old, from Suzhou), Yang Zhuzhu (12 years old, from Pinghu), etc. At 11 a.m. the day before yesterday, Yi Baozhu, Yi's cousin, suddenly reported to the French police, accusing Yi Fangshuo of rape and assault. They took Yi, along with his concubines Yi Caitao, Yi Meimei, Yi Didi, and all the young female performers, to the General Police Station. After a thorough investigation, it was discovered that Li Xiaozhen had also been raped twice, and Yi Baozhu had been raped as many as five times. The police chief immediately detained Yi. The plaintiff, Yi Zhuzhu, and Xiaozhen were temporarily kept outside the police station, and all the others were released. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Special District Court for questioning. At this time, Yi's legal wife arrived at the court with lawyer Zhu Honglie, also intending to join the accusation against Yi Fangshuo for rape, but she was dissuaded by relatives and friends. At 11 a.m., Judge Shan Chaozu ascended to the criminal court to conduct the hearing. He first questioned the defendant Yi Fangshuo about his age, origin, and address, and Yi stated that he lived in Shanghai with his mother, younger brother, and legal wife Jin Dasen, also known as Xu Guizhen, and that he had a daughter, named Sannan, who was 11 years old this year, and an adopted son who was 8 years old this year. He said that he currently performs comic dramas at Xinxin Company and earns 500 yuan per month. Next, he questioned the plaintiff Yi Baozhu, who stated, "The defendant is my cousin. My father and his father were brothers. I was adopted by my aunt when I was two or three years old, and when I was eight years old, my parents passed away. I came to Shanghai to the defendant's place on November 14th last year." Li Xiaozhen also stated, "I am 13 years old, and the defendant is my brother-in-law. Yi Meimei is my sister. I came to Shanghai to the defendant's place in August this year." At this point, police lawyer Yuan Jiahuang stood up and stated the facts of the case, briefly stating that the defendant was arrested for the crimes of disturbing public morals and restricting freedom. Currently, the police investigation is incomplete, so he requested a postponement and temporary detention of the defendant until the facts of the case are clarified and the case can be prosecuted. At the same time, he requested that the court temporarily send the two plaintiffs, the victims, to charitable organizations because they have no residence, until the case is adjudicated. The court acknowledged the report and, considering the case involved morality, announced that spectators were prohibited. After the spectators left, the judge began a detailed interrogation of the two plaintiffs, Yi Baozhu and Li Xiaozhen, and the defendant, Yi Fangshuo, which lasted for an hour before concluding. The court then ordered the case to be adjourned until the 21st for further hearing, and the defendant was remanded to custody. Yi Shizhu and Li Xiaozhen, after being sent to the forensic doctor for examination, would be sent back to the court for placement after the police investigation was completed. The court then adjourned. At 3 p.m., the two women were taken to the forensic lab by bailiffs. After the forensic examination, they were sent back to the court. After Judge Zhang inquired about the addresses of their hometown relatives, he ruled that Yi Baozhu and Li Xiaozhen should be temporarily detained at the court's detention center for investigation, pending a decision on the case, before being placed elsewhere.

Zhu Songshou's Life in Danger

A Pitiful Case of Neurasthenia

Zhu Songshou, from Anhui Province, thirty years old, formerly worked at the stamp tax bureau in Fengtian Province, Northeast China. As a result, Zhu swallowed more than ten sleeping pills before going to sleep the night before last, and soon fell asleep. However, at around 9 a.m. yesterday morning, Zhu's friend Wang Yi, who was staying in the same room, suddenly heard a moan, so he quickly got up to check and saw Zhu moaning in bed, unconscious, with blood flowing from his mouth and nose non-stop. Knowing that something unexpected had happened, he quickly reported to the front desk, who in turn reported to the Lao Zha Police Station, and Zhu was taken to the hospital for treatment. Although emergency treatment was given, his condition is critical, and his life is not yet guaranteed.

Russians Falsely Claiming Nationality Undermine Legal Authority 188

The Court and the Municipal Council Strictly Punish Such Actions

Shamenov's Scheme Ultimately Fails

In the past, when the legal rights of the concessions had not yet been recovered by our country, unscrupulous merchants would often claim foreign nationality in lawsuits and rely on foreign consuls as a shield to obtain various illegal conveniences. After the Mixed Court was abolished, the system of consular assessors was abolished, and our country established formal courts in the concessions, this trend of claiming foreign nationality in lawsuits disappeared. Unexpectedly, in recent years, the embers have gradually rekindled. When debtors are sued by creditors and the court renders a final judgment, such as when the court orders the seizure of their property, these people temporarily try to claim that their shops or properties have foreign capital or that they have claimed foreign nationality, in the hope of preventing enforcement. This kind of absurd act of borrowing foreign power to undermine the country's judiciary has recently spread to Russian nationals who have no consular jurisdiction. One person leads the way, and the masses follow suit. If such incidents are not closely monitored,

Serious Crackdown Needed 189

The impact will be profound, and the drawbacks will increase. The Legal Department of the Municipal Council is also deeply disgusted and resentful of this kind of fraudulent claim of nationality to avoid enforcement and undermine legal authority. For example, the recent incident of Russian Shamenov tearing down the seal of the First Special District Court that sealed his shop has been prosecuted according to law. This is because if this trend is allowed to continue, the consequences will be endless. The incident arose when Russian Shamenov, who opened the "Fumaina" silk shop at No. 940 Jing'an Temple Road, was sued by the German company Lianzhong Trading Company for owing money for goods. The First Special Court ruled against the plaintiff in the first instance on June 12th last year. The German company was not satisfied and appealed, and the Second Branch of the High Court ruled in favor of the plaintiff in the second instance, ordering the Russian to repay

Outstanding Debt 190

and interest. However, Shamenov claimed to be dissatisfied and filed a third appeal to the Supreme Court. The result was that Lianzhong Company ultimately won. After the third trial was finalized, the First Special Court approved Lianzhong's application and ordered the "Fumaina" shop to be sealed as collateral. On the 23rd of last month, a bailiff and police officer were specially dispatched

Seal 191

Together with the Jing'an Temple Police Station, the shop was sealed. Surprisingly, only five days after the sealing, Shamenov dared to secretly tear off the seal, break into the shop, and take all the goods stored in the shop. The police station was informed and sent detectives to investigate. The Russian suddenly claimed that the shop belonged to a Frenchman named Bascou. According to the landlord of the shop, the tenant "Fumaina" silk shop signed a lease agreement on October 1st of this year for a period of two years, but on October 15th, Shamenov, in the name of the Jinmei Silk and Satin Shop representative,

Lease Agreement 192

assigned the agreement to Frenchman Bascou. The police then investigated with the company that publishes the Shanghai name directory, the "Rossen Silk and Scrimshaw Forest Newspaper", and the China Credit Bureau, etc. Some entries listed the shop owner of "Fumaina" as Shamenov, and some only registered the shop name without the owner's name, but no connection between Bascou and the shop was found. It was also noted that when a Russian person accused Shamenov of criminal activity last winter on November 21st, the First Special Court ordered him to pay a security deposit of 1,000 yuan. When a police officer was dispatched to the shop to investigate, he also claimed that he was the sole owner of the shop. All these facts are sufficient to prove that the shop was indeed established by Shamenov. This

Sudden Change of Ownership 193

is to avoid the seizure, falsely claiming French nationality, and hoping to undermine our country's legal authority by not being subject to the jurisdiction of the First Special Court. The Legal Department of the Municipal Council believes that Shamenov's actions not only damage the creditor's rights but are also very serious in nature. Moreover, if this trend is allowed to continue, the consequences will be even worse. Therefore, lawyer Ru Baozhao, representing the bureau, filed a public prosecution against Shamenov, requesting punishment in accordance with Article 384 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday morning, Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special Court brought the defendant to court for questioning. First, lawyer Ru stated the intent of the prosecution, and then the defendant's defense lawyer said that they were currently negotiating a settlement with Lianzhong Company, hoping not to hinder the court's enforcement, and requested an extension. Lianzhong Company also invited lawyer Lin Yingqing to court and expressed their agreement to the defendant's request. Judge Huang then ordered Shamenov to be detained and adjourned the hearing for seven days. After this stern response, those who illegally change the ownership of property and rely on foreign power may be silenced.

Chinese Children

Outline of the Preparatory Committee

The Benevolent Infant Society Suggests to the Ministry of Education

The National Government previously required that the Republic of China be designated as Children's Year in 1935. The details have already been reported in this newspaper. However, the process of this event requires the National Government to organize a preparatory committee to gather the strength of the government and civil groups to lead the entire country in holding large-scale Children's Year celebrations. The Chinese Benevolent Infant Society of this port has already drafted an outline for the organization of this committee and the work items to be carried out, and has submitted it to the government for decision. It is reported that the draft outline for the organization of the Children's Year Preparatory Committee and the work items to be carried out are quite practical and detailed, and are therefore transcribed as follows:

1. Draft Outline of the Organization of the Chinese Children's Year Preparatory Committee: (1) Name: This committee shall be named the Chinese Children's Year Preparatory Committee. (2) Mission: The mission of this committee is to prepare for national substantive Children's Year affairs. (3) Organization: This committee shall be jointly organized by the Ministry of Education of the National Government, together with the Ministry of Interior, Chinese Children's Education Groups, Chinese Infant Welfare Groups, and Chinese Women's Groups. (4) Staff: This committee shall have one honorary chairman, one chairman, one vice chairman, and shall also establish general affairs, literary, economic, social, and publicity divisions for implementation. (5) Funding: The funding for this committee shall be allocated by the government. (6) Term: The term of office of this committee shall be from November 30, 1934, to December 21, 1935. (7) Supplementary Provisions: The detailed rules of procedure for this committee shall be determined separately.

II. Work Items of the Chinese Children's Year Preparatory Committee: (1) Publish a Chinese Children's Year Handbook. (2) Formulate Chinese Children's Year slogans. (3) Formulate Chinese Children's Year songs. (4) Formulate a Chinese Children's Year declaration (for use on January 1st). (5) Submit a request to the National Government to order all major and minor newspapers across the country to publish a special inaugural edition for Chinese Children's Year on January 1st. (6) Hold an inaugural ceremony for Chinese Children's Year in the capital (January 1st). (7) Hold a patriotic oath-taking ceremony for Chinese children in the capital (January 1st). (8) Broadcast lectures on children's happiness issues every Sunday via wireless radio. (9) Submit a request to the National Government to order all major and minor newspapers across the country to publish special editions on children's happiness every Sunday. (10) Collect and review children's toys from all over the country. (11) Collect and review children's books from all over the country. (12) Formulate a Chinese Children's Day song for the Ministry of Education to refer to. (13) Prepare for the audience ceremony of national children's representatives for the Chairman of the National Government (April 4th). (14) Hold a national children's calligraphy and painting competition. (15) Hold national children's sports games. (16) Hold national children's skill competitions. (17) Hold national children's speech contests. (18) Hold national children's concerts. (19) Hold a national arms exhibition. (20) Initiate national children's tours. (21) Compile a Chinese Children's Year report. (22) Other items.

Submission

What Kind of Policy Should China Adopt to Cope with World Changes? 197

Lecture by Zhang Yuanruo (Notes by Li Guangteng)

The Shanghai Educational Association is holding a broadcasting lecture to promote international knowledge. The first broadcast was given by political scholar Zhang Yuanruo, and his speech was very cautionary. The original manuscript is as follows: Ladies and gentlemen, I am very pleased to be invited by the Shanghai Educational Association to give a broadcasting lecture today. The topic I will be speaking on today is "What kind of policy should China adopt to cope with world changes?" The scope of this topic is very broad, and if I were to discuss it in detail, I would not have enough time today. I can only study the following two points:

I. An Overview of the Global Situation 198

Regarding when and where future global upheavals will occur, scholars, politicians, and diplomats hold differing opinions. Some say the center of future wars will be in Europe, while others claim they will erupt in the Far East. Both arguments have their rationale and possibilities. As for which, Europe or the Far East, will be first, I dare not make a definitive judgment. (I spoke in detail about the situation in Europe in 1936 at the YMCA; I encourage you to consult newspaper reports on that.) However, both regions are, in fact, powder kegs for future world wars, with the potential for war to break out at any moment. According to the American scholar Steel, the Second World War will originate from the contest for [missing characters] between two [missing characters]. In the Far East, it will stem from Japan's aggression against eastern Siberia. In my opinion, international relations are intricate, possessing an inseparable cyclical nature: the Far East is connected to Europe, and Europe is also connected to the Far East. Both regions are potential flashpoints for future world wars. Comparatively speaking, however, the explosiveness of the Far East is perhaps greater. The reasons are: 1. After the Great War, the center of world politics has shifted from the Atlantic to the Pacific. 2. The focus of major powers' interest struggles is now in the Far East. 3. Japanese militarists are ambitious and eager for recognition. Having not suffered the hardships of a major war, they are always looking to test their ambitions. According to recent news reports, Japan has unilaterally abandoned the naval treaty. This will naturally affect the balance of power in the Far East and symbolizes the increasing likelihood of a future world war. From this brief analysis of the global situation, we can infer how severely and dangerously we will be affected should a world war erupt in the Far East. This is the first point.

II. The Course We Should Take 199

The next question is: if a future world war breaks out in the Far East, which countries will be the main protagonists? Will it be Russia and Japan, or Japan and the United States? What will be the situation in the Far East, and what course should China take in this crisis to safeguard national survival? This can be briefly discussed in four parts: (A) I believe the main antagonists in the Far East will be Russia and Japan. Historically, they are historical enemies. The conflict of interests between them is more intense and acute than that between Japan and the United States. Since occupying Korea, Japan has been scheming to expand into Northeast China. Since the September 18th Incident, the conflict with Russia has intensified. Although the conflict between Japan and the United States is also severe, Japan has traditionally had two factions: the maritime policy faction and the continental policy faction. The target of the maritime policy faction is, of course, the United States. The target of the continental policy faction is, of course, Soviet Russia. Currently, Japan is focusing on the development of its continental policy, which is even more emphasized than its maritime policy, and Soviet Russia's military preparations are more intense than those of the United States. (B) Once a war breaks out in the Far East, before deciding on a course of action, we must carefully and thoroughly analyze the international situation and the interests of all parties involved to be able to cope with it adequately. We cannot definitively say what the situation will be after a major war erupts; it depends on a country's foreign policy. In other words, the situation is not entirely passive but can be shaped by us. According to Chang Hsiung, it is likely that a coalition of the United States and Russia against Japan may form. The reestablishment of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia proves the trend and possibility of a US-Russian alliance against Japan. As for Britain's foreign policy, it traditionally embraces a "wait and see" approach. We cannot easily grasp British foreign policy now because it is hesitant to express its position. In fact, the conflict of interests between Britain and Japan has become an open secret, which is discernible to those who understand international relations. Because the world is now capitalist, especially the "mercantilist" British Empire, it prioritizes economic interests. As everyone knows, the foundation of the British Empire is in the Far East, in India. If Japan were to dominate the Far East and the Pacific, it would inevitably shake the British Empire's outer line of defense in the Far East. Britain would be unable to maintain its base in India and would have to retreat to Suez. Wouldn't this be the collapse of the entire British Empire? Therefore, if a future war occurs in the Far East, there is a possibility of a US-Russian-British alliance. Some may argue that the conflict between Britain and the United States in the Far East is also significant. However, we must understand that although Britain and the United States inevitably have conflicts, if a war breaks out in the Far East, due to the geographical relationship of their colonies and the racial ties between them, they will ultimately unite and jointly resist Japan. (Regarding this point, please refer to the editorial by Gavin, the editor of the British Observer, and the Reuter's dispatch from London on November 3rd). (C) Now we must discuss what course China should take in this future global upheaval. Undoubtedly, our greatest enemy at present is Japanese imperialism. If we want to cope with this crisis, if we want to escape from death, the most important thing is to skillfully utilize the conflicts between Russia and Japan, Japan and the United States, and Japan and Britain to create a grand alliance of China, Russia, the United States, and Britain to restrain Japan. In this way, Japan will naturally be isolated in a "besieged on all sides" situation and will collapse on its own. (To be continued)

Letter to the Editor 201

The association's work is currently focused on raising funds, and the methods for soliciting designs and models are still being drafted. We will publicly solicit designs in newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai in the future, and no decisions have been made regarding the selection of candidates. I respectfully request that your newspaper correct this and publish the original letter. Sincerely, The Committee for Establishing the Sun Yat-sen Statue in the Capital. December 11th.

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and surrounding areas will have clear and cold weather with unstable winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River will have changeable weather with morning fog. Winds will be from the north to the east, and irregular due to a low-pressure system in Jiangxi. The East China Sea will be cloudy with [missing character] and gentle northeasterly to southeasterly winds. The Taiwan Strait will have northeasterly winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 58.1 degrees, and the lowest was 41.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 55.4 degrees, and the lowest was 34.7 degrees.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

Optimism for the Future of National Goods 203

— Yang An

For years, living in this time of national crisis, there have been few optimistic facts to report. Only the promotion of national goods has had some small effect. Everywhere you go, people feel that promoting national goods is morally right and that using them is everyone's duty. From the small clerk in a company to economic experts like Ma Yinchu, on the platform and in essays, they all say that the only way to save China, save the economy from national crisis, and reverse the outflow of silver is to promote and use national goods. In recent years, the consistent promotion of national goods has had some effect. You only need to go to a national goods company to see the crowds of male and female customers, and the batches of goods being manufactured in national goods factories, to feel a bit optimistic. Mr. Zhang Gongquan said in his speech at the China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association the other day: "The same ten months of import surplus, in 1932, was 690 million yuan, in 1933, it was 570 million yuan, and this year, 1934, it is only 150 million yuan. This cannot but be attributed to the effectiveness of promoting national goods. In the future, if everyone in the national goods industry cooperates, focuses on improving manufacturing, reducing costs, and urges the government to increase tariffs, and if those in the industry seek further integration, then the economic national crisis will be a good opportunity for the development of our national goods industry. Even the universally alarming silver tide can be solved by this." Mr. Zhang's optimistic words about the future of national goods indeed encourage the courage and enthusiasm of those in the national goods industry. I think comrades in the national goods industry will certainly be happy to accept these words and be willing to work hard.

National Goods Suggestions

Suggestions for (National Goods Year for Students) 204

— Xiao Bai

The wheels of time are constantly rolling forward. As the "National Goods Year for Women" is about to come to an end, the words "National Goods Year for Students" have already been written on the path of progress. Clearly, this is an indication of the tireless efforts of those promoting national goods. This year's failure will be harvested into next year's success. The so-called treatment of a five-year illness cannot be achieved in a single day. We should adhere to the spirit of continuous effort and perseverance to gradually make progress. At this time of bidding farewell to the old and welcoming the new, we should have grand plans and establish a strict plan and policy as a reference for future progress, seeking a way out of the darkness.

However, (the past can be a guide), as we continue to make persistent efforts, we should try our best to avoid repeating the mistakes of the past. We must understand why the "National Goods Year for Women" failed. In a word, it was because it did not work in a down-to-earth manner. In particular, the ladies and misses forgot their obligations and missions. Their fondness and worship of foreign goods did not change at all, making the staggering number of imported perfumes and cosmetics a concrete fact - a lesson of failure and pain for us.

Therefore, as the "National Goods Year for Students" is about to begin, (prevention is better than cure), we should first recognize that students are the most outstanding members of society, young people with ambition and potential. Their every move is enough to shift the attention of the entire nation, gaining importance and inspiring faith. The anti-goods movements of the May Fourth and May Thirtieth Movements are powerful evidence. Now, entrusting this responsibility to them to apply their skills will surely achieve (twice the result with half the effort). However, words alone are useless. We should have practical suggestions. Below, I will put forward two points based on my personal opinions, hoping that they will be adopted and implemented as soon as possible.

1. Schools should ban foreign goods. From New Year's Day next year, all schools nationwide should uniformly adopt national goods. All clothing, stationery, instruments, equipment, and all miscellaneous utensils must absolutely prohibit the use of foreign goods. Teachers and students should jointly organize a national goods usage committee to supervise each other and bear the responsibility of inspection. If violations occur on either side, the most severe punishment should be imposed.

2. Implement national goods education. The call for national goods education has been around for a long time, but it has not been implemented. However, next year, in the "National Goods Year for Students," it is necessary to implement it conscientiously. For example, regarding the reasons for using national goods and the knowledge of distinguishing national goods, it is best for the Ministry of Education to compile textbooks and order all schools to teach them, instilling them with knowledge. A national goods lecture series should be organized, and national goods celebrities should be invited to give lectures at schools during weekends and holidays to make it more interesting. In this way, I think next year's results will definitely be more satisfactory than this year's!

National Goods Talk

National Goods Advertising and Broadcasting 205

— Dao Qin

Modern advertising is advancing, changing with each passing day, and making rapid progress. Newspapers have newspaper advertisements, publications have publication advertisements, and there are even roadside and wall advertisements, and electric moving advertisements. In recent years, since the rise of radio, in large cities or areas with developed electrical industries, advertising has been broadcast. Residents only need to have a radio to listen, and even without leaving their homes, they can understand current affairs, international news, commercial situations, and the marketing of emerging products. It is truly a convenient and rapid tool for transmitting information.

Taking Shanghai as an example, there are no fewer than two hundred large and small broadcasting stations. Among them, only a few broadcast international news and current affairs. Most are for business purposes, specializing in broadcasting advertisements for factories and commercial firms. According to my usual observations, there are still few national goods manufacturers who entrust broadcasting, and only a few, such as Chinese and Western pharmacies that are self-prepared and family industrial societies that borrow from the Li Shutang Drugstore, are like phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. It is a pity that they have not been able to carry out large-scale, widespread publicity.

It must be said that in this era of commercial competition and foreign goods dumping, if our national goods factories do not implement the policy of small profits and quick sales, advertising, and publicity, they will not be able to consolidate their position and seek progress for the national goods industry. In my opinion, national goods manufacturers, in addition to newspaper and publication advertisements, should also broadcast on the radio according to the season or adapt to the environment and needs to promote the sales of their products, which can achieve twice the result with half the effort. I hope that those who have not joined will try it as soon as possible, and those who have already joined must consider the following two points:

First, when introducing the special qualities of a product, it must be explained that this quality is indeed superior to foreign goods and that the value is indeed cheaper than foreign goods. With the fluent and lively words of the broadcaster, making a pleasant and attractive publicity, the resulting attraction cannot be measured in distance.

Second, when introducing national goods products, foreign goods must be used as a comparison. For example, it can be said: "The Invincible Brand Tooth Powder of the Family Industrial Society can replace the Diamond Brand Tooth Powder of the enemy." "Invincible Brand Face Cream can replace foreign Palm Olive Cream and White Jade Cream." "The Double Dragon Brand Wool Yarn of the Zhenxing Woolen Mill can replace the Bee Brand Wool Yarn of foreign goods." "The Minsheng Brand Ink of the Minsheng Factory can replace the Stephens and Waterman Ink of foreign goods." "The Steel Plate of the Lizhong Copper File Factory can replace the stencil version of the enemy goods."......And so on, not only can it be used for advertising, but also to instill in people very good knowledge and concepts of distinguishing national goods and non-national goods. Isn't it a win-win situation?

Short Story

Country of No Goods 207

— Jin Jia

It is said that Duojiu Gong's ship sailed for many days. One day, the wind was calm and the waves were gentle. Tang Ao got up early and pointed to a piece of land in front and said, "I have been bored on the ship for days, and it is extremely boring. The food on the ship has been accumulating for a long time. If we don't reach the shore again, I am afraid it will not be enough for us to eat." So Duojiu Gong and others all leaned on the side of the ship. Lin Zhiyang asked Duojiu Gong where this was. Duojiu Gong shook his head and said, "I have traveled all over the famous seas and continents in those years, but I have never been here." Speaking of chatting, the wheel has already reached the shore, so all three of them came ashore.

The three walked on the shore. A man came in front, his appearance was like a Chinese person, but his clothes were very strange. The buttons were born in the center of the clothes, but the collar was turned down, the trousers were particularly long, and the shoes were also very strange, not made of silk, but made of black and hard things. Tang Ao was the first to go up, salute, and then asked, "What is your surname, sir, and what is this place called?" The man was very polite, but when he saw that they were wearing long gowns and cloth shoes, he seemed to despise them. On the one hand, he replied, "Brother Yang Hugao is just that, and my place is called the Country of No Goods. I don't know where you are from." Lin Zhiyang rushed to say, "We are Chinese, because we like to travel everywhere, so we brought Chinese goods to sell everywhere, so that we can broaden our horizons and make a few friends." The man seemed to be very happy. Tang Ao was also happy in his heart. Since this is the Country of No Goods, because he has no goods, he thinks that the goods on the ship today will definitely be sold.

Yang Hugao asked again, "Then what do you have?" Duojiu Gong said, "China has rouge, white powder, Huadiao, brown sugar, cloth, etc. What do you want, sir?" Who knew that Yang Hugao spit and said, "I almost took you for a fool. No one here wants these things. Do poor people even want to use rouge? Let me tell you! No one drinks Huadiao and other things. Foreign wine and white gate land are easy to promote. Speaking of clothes, the poorest people are willing to freeze to death rather than wear cloth. Look at me, a Paris satin shirt, a foreign tweed dress from Lailu, that's what you can wear. I don't have time to talk to you stubborn people, I'm going to join the preparatory meeting for promoting foreign clothes."

The three of them were inexplicable. They asked many people in a row, and they all said the same thing. Before they knew it, they were hungry, in a restaurant called Zhenzheng Old Brand Lailu Goods, and a piece of paper was posted on the window, which read; "If you use domestic goods to impersonate foreign goods, you will be fined 10,000 yuan." Thirteen words. Tang Ao entered the seat and asked the waiter, "I want to order Chennian Huadiao, and burn some local specialties." Who Qian waiter said, "Sir. Don't be kidding, these things can't be eaten here, or please go somewhere else!" It was still Duojiu Gong's wit, rushing to say, "Whatever you want, get some Lailu goods, and add some foreign wine! We don't understand the customs here." This made the waiter happy. Yibei said, "Do you want tea?" This time Tang Ao was also a little more obedient and said, "Is there Lailu tea? Get three cups." The waiter went happily.

After a while, the dishes, tea, and wine all came. Lin Zhiyang took a sip of tea and said, "It's terribly bitter." Tang Ao opened the wine bottle, but unexpectedly, there were bubbles inside, which scared the three of them and they didn't dare to eat. Speaking of dishes, instead of using chopsticks, they used forks, knives, and other things. Duojiu Gong and the other three had to grab it with their hands and eat it while the doctor was not there. Later, three pieces of bread and butter were sent up, and Lin Zhiyang felt that it was not very tasty. He didn't eat it either. The waiter took the bill, and the three of them were startled. It turned out that it was written on it.

After paying the money, they received a pack of chewing gum per person, which tasted not very good. The package was printed with "Four corners per piece four words. Duojiu Gong stretched out his tongue and didn't shrink back for a long time. The three of them discussed for a while, and seeing that this place was not a success, they had to go back to the ship. Lin Zhiyang bought another copy of the local newspaper. The important news contained a line of large characters; "The import of foreign goods this month reached 50 million yuan." It was noted next to it, "The national treasury is empty, and the people's wealth will be exhausted."

Duojiu Gong said, "The people admire foreign goods so much, how can the country not be poor, and how can the people not be poor?" Lin Zhiyang interjected, "That Yang Hugao, I know, is a homophone of foreign goods high. It can be seen that the people's psychology is general."

The ship of Tang Ao and the other three. It sailed again in the waves.

My Lover 208

— Wang Cen

After a long period of struggle and enduring much hardship, Kai and Ling's love finally succeeded.

The two of them are now planning to live together. The first thing to solve is the housing problem. They rented a side building near Zhaofeng Park on Yuyuan Road. Opening the window, they could see lush green trees and a flat lawn. They were very satisfied with the air of this residence. They also bought some simple appliances and daily necessities, and the conditions for a small family were ready. However, at this time, there was something that made them feel very inconvenient!

Because although Kai and Ling both had jobs, their monthly income was only enough for their expenses, and in fact, they could no longer afford to hire someone. Moreover, they were willing to do the housework themselves to realize a frugal life. The only problem was hot water. The reason was that there was no public bathhouse near their residence, and they could not go to a distant place to bathe themselves. They borrowed the landlord's stove for cooking and boiling water during the day. Sometimes when they needed hot water at night, the fire had already gone out! Especially as the weather gradually turned cold, Kai and Ling often felt a little unhappy about not having hot water when washing their faces before going to work in the morning!

One day, Kai came back from outside with a paper bag and said happily to Ling:

(Ling, we don't have to worry about hot water anymore.)

(Why?) Ling asked.

(I just went to the Wuzhou Pharmacy to buy this.) Kai said, opening the paper bag in his hand, which turned out to be a thermos.

(I thought about it a long time ago, but the price of foreign goods is very expensive!) Ling said.

(This is a top-quality domestic Earth brand thermos. The price is very economical, and the heat preservation effect is very accurate.) Kai said with a smile.

(Your design is very thoughtful. You are truly my lover!) Ling kissed Kai's face.

From then on, they had hot water to use, whether late at night or at dawn.

Little Western Paradise 209

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: The poor girl cannot be ashamed to take up teaching; how worthy is the Western tutor to empty his heart in vain.

As soon as he said the two words "Let's go", he had already walked over, supporting Yueying and asking her to turn around. As she turned around, guided by Aunt Hu, she saw that the student in the blue cloth clothes was still staring at her. In her haste, she had attracted the attention of such a person, which was something she had not expected. However, she was about to take the concubine test, which was a crucial moment of success or failure, and she had no time to worry about such idle matters. When Little Ji took them to the courtyard, he had already rushed ahead to inform Jia Duocai in his room. By the time he had delivered the message, he turned around and saw that no one was behind him, and he became very anxious. So, he turned around and ran back, jumping up and down as he saw Aunt Hu and saying, "Why are you walking so slowly?" Aunt Hu pushed Yueying and said, "She is shy." Little Ji said, "Mr. Jia said that you have already talked, so what's there to be shy about? But this is good, people will find it a bit more interesting." Yueying felt that what he said was simply inhuman, but at this time, she still had to rely on him for help, so she did not dare to contradict him, but blushed and walked with her eyes lowered. When they arrived at Jia Duocai's door, Little Ji rushed forward and lifted the door curtain for them to enter. As soon as they went in, he immediately put down the curtain and stood outside himself, not going in. Jia Duocai was sitting with his legs crossed, smoking a paper cigarette. When he saw them come in, his eyes were immediately absorbed by Yueying's brand-new clothes. He couldn't help but oh and ha, as if saying that it was too beautiful, unexpectedly beautiful. Yueying followed closely behind Aunt Hu, came in, and stood by the door with her head lowered. She was shy, and Aunt Hu was also shy. She took two steps forward and then two steps back. She did not speak to Jia Duocai, but pushed Yueying's shoulder and said, "Go over there, you already know each other, why are you suddenly shy?" (88)

Winter Sacrifice at Yamen to the Song Mother of the Nation 210

— Wang Yun

The Ci Yuan Temple in Yamen, a piece of land,

Still mourns for the soul of the nation with lingering sorrow!

Among the countries that have been oppressed by foreign tribes, none is more tragic than the Zhao Song! First subjected to the trampling of Liao and Jin, and then swallowed up by the Mongol Yuan, until Lu Xiufu carried Emperor Bing into the sea, the Song Dynasty's altars of state were destroyed in the great waves. When Empress Dowager Yang received the news of her son's death, she cried in pain, saying, "I endured hardship until now, just for a piece of Zhao's flesh! Now there is no hope!" Then she jumped into the sea and died. The Empress Dowager's palace is called Ci Yuan Temple. Later generations missed the Song Dynasty, and the temple enshrines Empress Dowager Yang, the mother of the Song Dynasty, which continues to this day.

At that time, Zhang Shijie, the Grand Preceptor who aspired to restore the country, still wanted to fight to the death after the defeat at Gaoting, and finally, the monarch died for the country, and the minister died for the monarch. His loyalty shines through the ages. His ancestral temple is in Yamen, called Da Zhong Temple, and also enshrines Wen Tianxiang and Lu Xiufu. This continues to this day.

Yamen is in the vast sea south of Xinhui County. Two mountains stand like doors, and the tide ebbs and flows between them, with a magnificent landscape. After the emperors of the Song Dynasty threw themselves into the sea and died, the surviving members of the Zhao clan entered Xinhui, and their descendants are still thriving today. Last month (November 22nd) was the date of the Zhao clan's winter sacrifice to the Song Dynasty's mother of the nation in the Yamen Ci Yuan Temple. In advance, the Zhao clan members from Sanjiang Xiaolu and other villages prepared taro offerings and hired a number of civilian ships to carry the elderly Zhao clan members to the sacrifice (mourning for the Song Dynasty's mother of the nation, Yang, who died for a piece of flesh). On that day, County Magistrate Huang Huaitting, Commissioner Fan Guoyan, and President of the Xinhui Local Court Li Mingding all went to participate in the sacrificial ceremony. They crossed the sea and traveled south, and after arriving at the port, each of the officials took on the role of chief priest. County Magistrate Huang presided over the Ci Yuan Temple sacrifice, Commissioner Fan presided over the Da Zhong Temple sacrifice, and President Li presided over the sacrifice to the shrines of various righteous people who died before the restoration was completed. The ceremony was solemn, and the entire venue was solemn. The ceremony concluded at about 2 p.m., and the participants dispersed separately. As the saying goes, "Remember the past and learn from it." Now that the national humiliation is heavy and resembles the external humiliation of the Southern Song Dynasty, officials sacrificing to the Song Dynasty's mother of the nation and the shrines of the righteous people of the Da Zhong Temple can also awaken the national spirit and take the Zhao Song as a lesson. According to the Zhao clan members, "This kind of grand three-offering sacrifice was held once during the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. It has been almost thirty years since then, and only now is there a second grand sacrifice. If the mother of the nation knows, she will surely be grateful in heaven. It goes without saying that we clan members are moved to tears."

The Tragedy of Actors 212

— Xun Zi

The name of the famous actor in the theater is written in large gold letters on the sign, and many electric lights are installed on all sides. Every night, there are horses, carriages, and flowing crowds, and everyone is vying to listen to his performance. Enquire about his performance fee, and it is at least two or three thousand yuan a month. In the eyes of the general public, it seems that they should live luxuriously and comfortably, but who knows that this is not the case!

There is a civil and military old actor with a performance fee of two thousand yuan a month. He is the top performer in the theater. He has no hobbies and does not fool around outside. Who knows that he is always in debt! When he really has no other choice, he has to send entire boxes of costumes to the pawnshop! What is the reason for this after all? It turns out that he was idle for ten months before this performance, so he was short more than five thousand yuan. This time he is performing, he must first repay his debts. In addition, he owes five or six thousand to the costume shop. Moreover, the so-called famous actor needs to provide for the families of the musicians, drummers, and supporting actors in martial arts performances, a total of ten or so families, relying on this famous actor to provide. Since he is the top performer, he cannot be sloppy with his costumes. A coat costs eighty yuan, and a python robe costs one hundred and twenty. Each month, adding new costumes costs at least three to five hundred yuan. For all these reasons, although he is earning such a large performance fee, he is always living on the verge of bankruptcy!

This civil and military old actor has a quirk. No matter how difficult things are at home, when he sees something he loves, he must spend money to buy it back. During the January 28th Incident, the theater where he was performing burned down, and all the servants at home were eating pancakes every day. Finally, a certain celebrity gave him one hundred yuan. Logically, he should go back and buy rice and firewood! Who knows that the old man was carrying one hundred yuan in his arms, walked past an antique shop, saw a precious sword that could cut iron like mud, and he had to buy it. He spent eighty yuan to buy the sword home, and his family had to continue to starve. Because he has this kind of temperament, no matter if his performance fee is increased to eighteen thousand, his economic situation will never improve!

Another Tan-style old actor is young, but he has taken up opium smoking. It is said that because old Tan used to smoke opium, if those who learn from him do not smoke, their singing will not be flavorful enough. This is certainly his excuse, but in the singing profession, there are really quite a few comrades in the underworld. The more years they have, the greater their opium addiction. If they ever fall out of favor, their performance fee drops, or they are idle for a year and a half, that will be the end of them!
