Trivial Jottings 214

— (Mei Ping)

When I saw barbers and masseuses on Sichuan Road, at first I mistakenly thought they were gilded medical doctors and nurses, because they were all wearing white coats outside their clothes.

The owner of the building opposite my residence used the national flag of the party-state as a door curtain. Perhaps he did not intend to insult the national flag of the party-state, but was the only believer in the Kuomintang. Otherwise, why would he even ask it to supervise when making little citizens? That is how I feel.

Once, my close relative surnamed Li, who was very honest, got married. On the way to the banquet, I mistakenly remembered Wangping Street Fuxing as Pingwang Street Xingyuan. I didn't realize it until I had eaten half of the feast, because it just so happened that this family was also surnamed Li.

Small Gardening

On Oranges 215

— Lü Mengjiao

The orange is an evergreen shrub, cultivated in the Jianghuai area of China, as well as in the provinces of Hunan, Guangdong, Fujian, and Zhejiang. The trunk is over ten feet tall, with white flowers blooming in autumn and bearing fruit in early winter, with colors ranging from yellow to green. It is full of sweet liquid, which is sweet and refreshing to eat. Su Dongpo's poem to Liu Jingwen says, "When lotus leaves have withered and lost their sheltering shade, Chrysanthemums still flaunt their frost-defying sprays. Remember well this finest time of year; When oranges turn yellow and tangerines turn green.” I feel that in this season, I cannot help but write about this wonderful fruit, so I present this discourse on oranges.

Previous scholars have written extensively on chrysanthemums, crabs, peonies, and the like, but only a few have written about oranges. Only Han Yanzhi of the Song Dynasty wrote three volumes on oranges. Yanzhi was from Yan'an, the eldest son of Zhongwu, King Shizhong. He passed the imperial examination in the tenth year of Shaoxing and became a scholar of the Longtu Pavilion. This book was written when he was the prefect of Wenzhou during the Chunxi period. The first volume contains eight varieties of tangerines, one variety of oranges, with the milk tangerine of Nishan at the top. The middle volume contains eighteen varieties of oranges. The last volume speaks of methods of planting. Later, Chen Jingyi's "Quan Fang Bei Zu" also touched on oranges, but it was not a dedicated work.

Both tangerines and oranges belong to the citrus family, but they are not exactly the same. However, they are often mixed up. For example, in Fujian, they are called tangerines, while in Guangdong, they are called sweet oranges, and honey oranges are called tangerines. Therefore, there is a saying, "Tall oranges, flat tangerines," as detailed in the Xinhui Zhi. In fact, tangerines are yellowish-red, while oranges are pure yellow. Tangerine peel is fine and tight, and difficult to peel, while orange peel is rough and easy to peel. Tangerines are sweet, while oranges are sour. There are differences between them.

The best oranges are produced in Zhejiang, not Fujian, and Yongjia in Zhejiang is the best. The "Qun Fang Pu" says, "Oranges from Suzhou, Taizhou, west from Jingzhou, and south from Fujian, Guangdong, and Fuzhou, are all not as good as Wenzhou." The "Oujiang Yi Zhi" says, "Yongjia is suitable for oranges, and the leaves are upright, as Ye Zhengze's poem says, 'There are orange trees in every forest, and lotus flowers in every water.'" Their flavor is extremely sweet, with those without seeds being the best.

Nishan is in Pingyang County, only three or two miles long, and is famous for producing milk tangerines. The "Qun Fang Pu" says that the tangerines of Nishan taste like milk, hence the name. Its trees are graceful, its branches are slender, its flowers are fragrant, its fruits are round and upright, its skin is like glazed wax, its size is six or seven inches, its skin is thin and its flavor is precious, its veins do not stick to the segments, and it leaves no residue when eaten. One fruit has only two or three seeds, and some have none at all. When broken open, a fragrant mist sprays out, making it the best among tangerines.

The "Quan Fang Fo Zu" distinguishes five varieties of oranges: orange, pomelo, fragrant pomelo, kumquat, and trifoliate orange. Oranges produced in Xinhui, Guangdong are the best, which are commonly known as Xinhui oranges. Its top has a pattern like a circle, which the locals often use to distinguish authenticity.

During the reign of Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty, an orange official was established in Jiaozhi to manage the tribute of imperial oranges. During the Wu and Yue periods, an orange register was established again. Wu Ji Ze said, "Please remove my orange register," as seen in "Shu Yi Ji."

The orange fruit has fibrous tissue, winding around the peel, which is called orange fiber. Both the peel and the fiber of the orange can be used in medicine.

There are also smoked oranges, which the "Ju Lu" says: "If the orange shows damage, then remove the peel, place the flesh segments in the space, and smoke it with fire, called smoked orange. Soak it in sugar and honey, and its taste is even better."

The cultivation of oranges attaches great importance to soil quality. If the soil flavor is different, even transplanting good seeds will be useless. Therefore, Yan Zi said that if an orange grows in Huainan, it will be an orange, but if it grows in Huaibei, it will be a trifoliate orange. The leaves are similar, but the taste is different. Now, when we say that relocation is not good, we often say "oranges that have crossed the Huai River," which is where the meaning comes from.

There are many good poems about oranges. Ye Shi's "Orange Branch Song" says, "Honey fills the room, gold for skin, short days in people's homes hang sparse fences, judge frost and cut dew to load the boat, don't sing 'Yang Branch Song,' sing 'Orange Branch Song.'" Su Zhe's poem "Gui Jun Sends Warm Tangerines" says, "The yellow tangerines of Chu Mountain are small as bullets, I have not seen the three-inch tangerines of Dongting, if there were no elegant guests from Wu and Yue, who would send them thousands of miles to the south of the Yangtze River?" Sentence fragments such as Fang Weng's "Green buds and leaves pluck new oranges," Zheng Yuanyou's "Ripe oranges, yellow fragrance presses the branches low," and You Wenjing's "Oceans, western winds, oranges, and pomelos are fragrant" are all charming and lovely.

Records of Fleeting Incense 216

— Original by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Tongzhi was the eighth emperor of the Qing Dynasty, and he was the Empress Dowager's own son. Unfortunately, this little emperor died too early. He only lived for nineteen years before dying of a severe case of smallpox. This was naturally very heartbreaking for the Empress Dowager!

Although Tongzhi occupied such a short period of time, he could not be said to have made any contributions to the country's economy or people's livelihood. Even his literary and military talents must have been very limited. However, his relics have been collected quite a lot, far exceeding those of his poor father, Emperor Xianfeng. Perhaps this is because he was still a child, and he liked everything, and he already owned a large part of treasures and supplies during his lifetime, so he left so many behind after his death. Or perhaps it was not like this, but because the Empress Dowager loved him too much, and could not bear to let him be forgotten because he had not accomplished anything, so she took extra care to collect his relics and send them to these ancient palaces, hoping to let him borrow the power of these things to win an immortal name.

When she arrived at this palace, the Empress Dowager had transformed into a compassionate mother full of sorrow. The first thing that caught her eye was a square glass box. Inside was a small bowl made of pure gold, with a very light style. Although it was gold, it would not look heavy at all. It was also engraved with many delicate patterns and auspicious words. This was the rice bowl that Tongzhi used during his lifetime. Stored with this rice bowl was a small silver scale. In those days, the Empress Dowager used this scale to personally prepare food for Tongzhi every day, so as to prevent him from eating too much or not enough.

In another larger glass box, we also saw a small dragon robe that Tongzhi wore when he was on the throne. (198)

Provisional Meeting of the Sino-Polish Cultural Association 221

Welcoming Honorary Presidents

Farewell to Polish Members

The Sino-Polish Cultural Association held a provisional tea party at its office at 5 pm on the 11th to welcome honorary presidents Cai Yuanpei and Wu Zhihui, and to bid farewell to Polish members Wieraszki and Wit-Norski returning to their country. Those present included honorary president Cai Yuanpei (Wu Zhihui sent a letter saying that he could not attend due to a cold), as well as members Okinczyc and his wife, Wieraszki, Wit-Norski (Polish members), Yuan Xiayi, Chen Shaokang, Yu Binglie, Guo Youshou, Xie Shoukang, Zhang Yuanchang, Tang Yiren, Chen Yaodong, Chu Anping, Lei Zhen, Hu Tieyan, Chen Jianxiu, Li Jiaxiang, Huang Jianzhong, Xie Jianhua, Tang Xueyong, Guo Lianfeng, Yuan Junmu, Wu Shuchang, Xu Beihong, Liu Hou, Liao Jianan, Xiong Wenmin, Zhang Shuqi, Jiang Biwei, Zhang Tong, Zhai Junqian, Gao Chengyuan, Li Shengwu, Hang Liewu, Li Jingbi, Dai Ce, Peng Xuepei, (Chinese members), and more than thirty others. First, Director Xie Shoukang gave a speech, stating that the establishment of the association was deeply indebted to the guidance and support of the two honorary presidents, Cai Zimin and Wu Zhihui, but because the two gentlemen were not often in Nanjing, the members of the association had few opportunities to receive their teachings in person. Today, Mr. Wu was unable to come due to a cold, but Mr. Cai personally came to the meeting to give guidance. Mr. Cai is a leading figure in the academic world and needs no introduction. On behalf of the members, I express my welcome and gratitude. But today there is also a report, that is, the Polish members of the association, Mr. Wit-Norski and Mr. Wieraszki, will soon return to their hometowns. We take this tea party as an opportunity to bid farewell. The two gentlemen have been very enthusiastic about the association's affairs, and the association relies on them deeply. Hearing that their departure is near is deeply regrettable. Now, I will introduce the brief histories of the two gentlemen, Wei and Wei. The two gentlemen are young Polish scientists with a very promising future. Both were born in 1905, Wei was from Wołow and Wei was from Krakow. Both studied at the world-renowned Krakow University. In 1930, Wei obtained a doctorate in medicine from Wołow University, and Wei obtained two doctoral degrees in medicine from Poznań University a year earlier. During their studies, they represented the Medical Student Federation and went to Romania, Turkey, France, Italy, Spain, Austria, the Czech Republic, and other countries to connect with students from various countries and promote the exchange of students to promote mutual understanding and cultural exchange between countries. The two gentlemen also have very rich medical experience. Wei Min served as an obstetrician at Wołow University Hospital and a doctor at the Krakow Infectious Disease Hospital, and also served as a government doctor in the Polish-Russian border area. Wei Shi served as a surgeon at Wołow University Hospital, a doctor at the Krakow Infectious Disease Hospital, and a doctor at the largest mental hospital in Poland (with 1,500 beds). Both Wei and Wei have traveled to the UK and the US. The two gentlemen share the same ideals and have consistent standpoints and opinions in science. They are both enthusiastic about researching medical psychology, and pay special attention to various issues of psychopathology. In order to study the relationship between social conditions and psychopathology, they decided to come to Asia to conduct on-site investigation and experimentation. In June 1932, they departed from Poland, passing through Romania, Russia, Turkey, to reach Persia. They stayed in Persia for seven months and were allowed by the King of Persia to establish a clinic in Siraz. Because they could speak Persian, they were able to approach the Persian people. From Persia, they took a car to India, passing through the southern Iranian plateau and the Balochistan desert. They traveled in India for five months, visiting mental hospitals, studying the system of religion and philosophy, and learning about the outline of old-fashioned medicine. Then they passed through Ceylon, Penang, Singapore, Saigon, Hong Kong, to reach Shanghai, in June of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. At first, they contacted the Chinese Medical Association, and then served as a psychiatrist at the Suzhou Mental Hospital for one month. Starting this year, the Examination Yuan hired Mr. Wit-Norski as the chief medical officer of the Health Department of the Yuan, and Wieraszki as a health consultant. Wei Shi traveled north for three months and worked in the neurology department of the Xiehe Hospital for several weeks, and visited the ophthalmology hospital of the Polish Church in Shunde Prefecture. Wei Shi accompanied President Dai Jitao and the Panchen to Hangzhou in the summer. Now, when the two gentlemen leave Nanjing for North China this week and go to Japan and the Americas for about half a year before returning to Poland to work in mental hospitals, in addition to the two members' grand tour around the world, it is hoped that they will bring back goodwill towards the association and China, promote the purpose of the association in Poland, and help as much as possible. At this time of farewell, I cannot help but feel reluctant. I wish the two gentlemen a safe journey. Then Cai Yuanpei gave a speech, briefly saying that he had participated in many works during the preparation of this meeting, and today he participated in this grand meeting and bid farewell to Wei and Wei, which is very happy. The association has already achieved a certain scale for the work of communication between Chinese and Polish cultures, and plans to have various publications and lecture plans, which is very rare. There are many things to be done in the future, and we should do our best to develop the cultural undertakings of the association. Then Wieraszki replied, saying that he was very happy to participate in today's event. The comrades came to China for a year and a half, not for business or office, but for the purpose of studying psychopathology. Living here for a long time, I feel that the Chinese nation is upright and peaceful, and its temperament is great. It nurtures a long-standing culture. With the strength of the Chinese people, it will contribute greatly to the world culture in the future. Although Poland is a newly emerging country, it also pays great attention to the promotion of cultural and academic undertakings. With this meeting, mutual assistance or a slight effort can be made. I am very grateful for the grand intentions of today's gathering. Then Wit-Norski said that various international organizations now have the purpose of eliminating world wars and seeking world peace. Although this association may not have such great power, but if we treat each other with sincerity, we can at least increase the degree of mutual understanding between the two countries, and seek the communication of culture between the two countries, which will indirectly contribute to the maintenance of world peace. The guests and hosts chatted happily over tea and snacks until after 7 pm before the meeting adjourned.

Regular Meeting of the Chinese Institute of Engineers 226

Ling Zhuming Lectures on the Yuehan Railway Project

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers held the first regular meeting of the 23rd year at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club at 7 pm on the 8th. More than 40 people attended. After the gathering, Xu Peihuang, the former president, reported on the financial situation of the branch. Yan Liping and Qiu Xieyun were designated to review the report. Then the new staff of this session was held. As a result, Xu Shanxiang was elected as the president, Wang Shengshan as the vice president, Shi Konghuai as the secretary, and Feng Baoling as the accountant. However, Shi Konghuai resigned due to personal affairs, and now Xu Mingcai will be appointed to replace him. Secondly, the general association is currently raising donations to purchase materials and testing equipment. Please help the branch to help. Then, the new president was invited to preside over the speech, and then the preparatory committee for the New Year's Friendship Conference was designated. Wang Shengshan was the director of the preparatory committee, Feng Baoling and Zhu Shuyi were the deputy directors of the preparatory committee, and Jin Zhixuan, Huang Yan, Yang Ximou, Xue Cixin, Xu Peihuang, Lu Chengzhang and others were the directors of each sub-group. Then, Ling Zhuming, director of the Zhushao Section Engineering Bureau of the Yuehan Railway, was invited to lecture on the engineering situation of the section. He briefly said that the Yuehan Railway has a history of 38 years. The northern section is the Xiang'e Road, built with British loans, 417 kilometers long. The southern section is the Guanshao Road, built by the Yuehan Railway Company, 224 kilometers long. The section from Shaozhou to Zhuzhou is more than 450 kilometers long and has been suspended for 15 years. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Railways planned to use the British Boxer Indemnity to complete this road, and first built the section from Shaozhou to Lechang, which is 51 kilometers long, with funds raised by the Ministry. It was completed in August 22nd. At the same time, it borrowed the British Boxer Indemnity to build the section from Lechang to Zhuzhou. Detailed measures have also been negotiated. It is estimated that 1.66 million pounds of Boxer Indemnity will be used for purchasing materials in the UK, and 31 million yuan of national currency will be used for labor and material costs in the country. The section is 407 kilometers long. The engineering bureau is located in Hengzhou, and the project is divided into seven general teams, a total of 21 teams, with a total of more than 58,000 workers. It will proceed in three directions from Lechang to the north, Hengzhou to the south, and Zhuzhou to the south. It was originally scheduled to complete the entire section of the project in April 26th, and later changed to the end of 25th. According to the current situation, it is expected that the entire line can be opened to traffic in the summer of 25th. The maximum slope of the section is set at 1.285%, which is the smallest curve of 240 meters compared to the 1.5% used by the Pinghan and Longhai railways. The section has a total of 16 tunnels, the longest is more than 400 meters, and the shortest is about 100 meters. There are three large iron bridges with a maximum span of 60 meters. There are many copper-reinforced concrete arch bridges with spans ranging from 30 meters to 40 meters. The section passes through many mountains, the terrain is steep, and transportation is difficult. At the same time, the road is relatively remote, and it is not easy to find contractors. After the workers have been found, the issues of accommodation and food are particularly difficult, and the bureau is trying to solve them. The section uses 85-pound steel rails. The design of the bridge is based on the Kubal E500 combat weight. Part of the sleepers are supplied by Canada and part by Australia. All have been treated with preservatives. In the future, Hunan may be able to supply a part of pine and fir. After each section of the project is completed, it will be opened to traffic immediately. It has been stipulated to use 484 locomotives, with a load capacity of Kubal E37.5. The bridge load capacity of Xiang'e Road is Kubal E40, and Guanshao Road is E45. Therefore, the locomotives that have been determined can be used throughout the Yuehan Road in the future. The determined vehicles are 40-ton steel cars. Hunan produces coal and rice, which can be supplied to Guangche after the opening of traffic. The economic development prospects are unlimited. After the lecture, the members praised Ling Jun as the former director of the Lingtong Section Engineering Bureau of the Longhai Railway, who has achieved outstanding results. This time, he is in charge of the most great, most important, and most difficult project of the Zhushao Section, and he is able to handle it with ease. Among the railway construction engineers in our country, there are Zhan Tianyou, who built the PingSui Railway, and Ling Zhuming, who is currently building the Longhai Railway and the Yuehan Railway. They all expressed their respect and asked detailed questions and discussions with great interest. The meeting ended after 11 o'clock.

Academic Lecture by the University Education Association 227

Yesterday, Han Juemin lectured at the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts

The academic lecture organized by the Shanghai University Faculty Association and the Professor Writers Association was given by Han Juemin, a lecturer of the association and a professor at the National Shanghai Business School, at the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts yesterday afternoon at 3 pm. The topic was "How to Revive the Chinese Nation", which was divided into what is the nation, the reasons for decline, and the methods of revival. The topic was very rich and meaningful. It lasted for an hour before it was completed. Recent News from Suyan City Senior Vocational School

Since Jiangsu Provincial Yancheng Middle School was reorganized into an Applied Chemistry program this semester, there have been significant improvements in equipment and curriculum. At a time when production education is being promoted, the recent situation of the school is presumably of great interest to the public. A brief overview is provided below:

(1) Three-Year Plan Drafted: Since being ordered to establish the Applied Chemistry program, the school immediately began drafting a three-year plan. The main subjects of this plan are the production of refined salt and the electrolysis of salt. Yancheng is located by the sea and is originally a salt-producing area, making the production of refined salt and the electrolysis of salt most suitable. In addition to the electrolysis of salt, which can produce caustic soda, bleaching powder, hydrochloric acid, and magnesium carbonate, the school also plans to focus on brewing as a subsidiary subject, engaging in the production of wine, soy sauce, MSG, and other products. Recently, Principal Wu of the school, in order to enrich the equipment and facilitate student practice, has submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for approval to allocate a large sum of money to build a factory in the second semester of this year for analytical testing and manufacturing purposes. On the other hand, he suggested that students from all chemical vocational schools in the province should rotate and exchange practical experience, so as to learn from each other's strengths and make up for their own weaknesses. It is said that this suggestion has been sympathized with by various schools.

(2) Holding Scientific Lectures: In order to increase students' interest in science, the school held a scientific lecture on December 1st. The topics were determined by the teachers, and the students were allowed to choose their own speakers. In addition to two representatives from each grade, there was also enthusiastic participation from those who volunteered. It is said that during the lecture, each speaker elaborated in detail and was very engaging.

In addition, the school is vigorously implementing the New Life Movement. All classrooms, dormitories, and public places are cleaned by the entire faculty and students in designated areas after breakfast to cultivate students' work habits. Other aspects, such as student etiquette and language, are also examined at any time. The whole school spirit is quite uplifted.

Road Bureau Actively Prepares for Qingyang Port Rowing Competition 229

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, considering that Qingyang Port has always been a venue for foreign boat races, which are grand events every spring and autumn, and that the scenery is beautiful and a popular outing destination, will establish a railway garden hotel there this spring and plan to organize a Chinese rowing club to provide recreation and exercise for people from all walks of life. Since hearing about it, it has been praised by Chinese and foreign people and appreciated by the Shanghai education and sports circles. Regarding the rowing organization, the Shanghai China Boy Scouts have been invited to hold a competition on a scheduled date to promote rowing. With four people per team, the report participants include 32 teams of male Boy Scouts and 8 teams of female Boy Scouts. It has been decided that Saturday, December 16, will be the day of the competition, with the preliminary round at 9:30 am and the final round at 1:30 pm. The Road Bureau will provide special treatment for visitors, and student groups of ten or more will receive a 50% discount on ticket prices. For those traveling from Shanghai, the third-class fare is only 65 cents per person. Meals will be provided by the Qingyang Port Railway Hotel at a 30% discount on the list price. The departure times from Shanghai North Station are 7:17 am (special train), 9:00 am, and 11:00 am, for a total of three trains. The return times from Qingyang Port to Shanghai are 4:26 pm, 5:22 pm, 6:00 pm (special train), 6:44 pm, and 9:24 pm, for a total of five trains. If there are a particularly large number of people, additional trains will be arranged temporarily. The travel time is about one hour.

Sixth International University Games 231

To Be Held in Hungary Next Year

The sixth International University Games, organized by the International Student Sports Federation, are now scheduled to be held in Budapest, the capital of Hungary, in September next year. In addition to holding the Games, Budapest University will also hold a 300th-anniversary celebration. At that time, there will be a very grand celebration. The Preparatory Committee of the Conference was held in London in early November this year, and the schedule and items of the conference have been discussed and announced as follows:

(1) Rowing: September 10 to 11

(2) Swimming: September 10 to 12

(3) Fencing: September 11 to 17

(4) Track and Field: September 15 to 18

(5) Soccer: September 10 to 18

In addition, the schedules for basketball and rugby have not yet been determined. Women's events include track and field, fencing, tennis, and swimming. In addition, the distance medley relay event in track and field has been decided to be abolished. As for whether individual or team competitions in gymnastics will be included, it has not yet been decided.

After Seven Consecutive Days of Declines, Gold Bar Prices Slightly Rebound 234

Customs Gold Unit Shrinks, Pressure Still Present

Struggles Result in a Slight Improvement of Three Cents

The gold market has been falling sharply for days, and yesterday it finally rebounded slightly. Although sentiment showed a rebound, short sellers slightly covered their positions. However, because many parties were still settling their positions, large players continued to exert pressure, and the situation in the first half of the day was very tense. Swaps are urgent, and floating longs should be gradually liquidated. The remaining buyers are probably well prepared, and the trend may temporarily stabilize. It was found that in the early morning, the overseas silver market rose in both the UK and the US, and the forward silver market rebounded by 4.5 cents. Exchange rates shrank slightly, and London spot gold was stable, so sentiment was still stable. In off-market preparatory transactions, the opening price once rose to 70 yuan and some odd cents. It was rumored that the central bank's listed Customs Gold Unit would shrink by 2 cents, and although it fell to 67 yuan, it still rebounded. However, sentiment had already been startled, and the opening was even lower in the morning. The central bank's listed exchange rates were announced: the British pound rose by 1.25, and the US dollar rose by 1.875. The Customs Gold Unit plummeted by 1.5 cents, and the standard gold bar price also fell to 1,003.2 yuan. Sentiment was greatly frightened, and a selling frenzy began. After the opening, it immediately fell to 64.5 yuan. However, sentiment rebounded at the low, and large players bought in unison. After that, buyers actively moved in, gradually pulling up the price, which actually rebounded to beyond the 70 yuan mark. Sassoon aggressively offered shillings, and the HSBC exchange rates also rose by 1.25 for the British pound and 1.875 for the US dollar. They took advantage of the high to supply sources and fell back. Large short players, such as Tongfengheng and Yuanyi, aggressively sold bars, frequently exerting pressure, and fell again after the rise. However, foreign short-term financing loosened, and sentiment had calmed down. Those who maintained the low price were very strong. The silver equalization tax was announced unchanged, still levying 6.75%. The British exchange rate was calculated at 1 shilling, 5 pence, and 65625. After that, the situation returned to stability, and in-market transactions were in greater demand than supply, gradually rising to beyond 70 yuan. The exchange market was slightly tight, and sentiment was originally good, so the upward trend started again. However, those who supplied at high prices became more active, and after the high, prices gradually fell. Sassoon still had a selling appetite, floating longs wavered, and large players also cut their long positions. There was once a correction, but the exchange market had settled down and was difficult to change. After a low, there were buyers, and transactions were small. Although there was another rise, Yuanyi sold bars again, and the situation at noon settled down. It was a small rebound after seven consecutive days of declines. The total number of lots was more than 28,000. Now, the market situation in the first half of the day is recorded below.

The morning opening was 966 yuan, down 3.7 yuan from the previous close. During the first session, supply and demand were balanced, and the price hovered around 6 yuan. Knowing in advance that the HSBC exchange rates were up 1.25 for the British pound and 1.875 for the US dollar, Dafa and Yongdingtai took advantage of the high price to sell, retreating to 69.6 yuan. Hengyu, Shunmao, Qianchang, Xiangfu, Changdafa, and Yong also advanced, and the price rose back to 70.09 yuan. Near and Far-Term Market Prices Have Converged

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, although foreign interbank lending rates eased by four fen, the market price showed no improvement and instead moved downward. The rebound from the closing price the day before yesterday was only a fleeting moment. The market price gradually weakened, and the abnormal situation of near and far-term market prices converging still appeared, and it became increasingly close, even to the point where the far-term exceeded the near-term. This kind of irregular anomaly occurred after the September 18th Incident due to the urgency of funds, but its abnormality was far different from the present. It will only be able to recover when the current foreign exchange returns to the norm. Therefore, although the environmental situation is good, arbitrage trading is still rare, and the market price is struggling to rise. The future is still temporarily in a downward curve. Yesterday's experience: the opening price in the morning seemed to have an upward trend, but the military reorganization bonds only improved by two or three jiao, and people's hearts were therefore discouraged. Starting from the 20th bond, it fell due to the selling of 53rd bonds, so the subsequent listings were lower by two or three jiao. In the second round, people's hearts turned weak, and there was also selling of the 16th bond, and the market price trended downward severely. The gold short bond fell sharply by six jiao and a half. The opening price in the afternoon was slightly chaotic, with highs and lows alternating. Although the 4th bond had purchases from five fen one jiao to two jiao and a half, it still felt weak. According to the late evening news, the situation in the Pacific was gradually rising, which originally had a rebound, but was hit again, and continued to decline by two or three jiao. Although there is a rebound in the future, it may not be easy to restore its original state. The market price result was a drop of one or two jiao to seven or eight jiao. The trading volume was extremely high, totaling 3.845 million yuan. The results of its rise and fall are listed in the comparison table on the left (unit: yuan).

Sudden Downturn in New York Stock Market 236

The New Fung Foreign Exchange reported that the New York stock market experienced a sudden downturn in the last half hour yesterday (the 11th), with each stock falling by one to four yuan or more. Trading was brisk, and the telegraphic transfer machines were overwhelmed. Initially, trading was light and prices trended slightly weaker, but the situation suddenly took a sharp turn for the worse. Large transactions of 1,000 to 5,000 shares were sold off one after another, and the downward trend was also fierce. The reason for the sudden crash is still unclear. It may be because traders were disappointed that railway stocks could not maintain their rise. The Roose film initially experienced a downturn due to rumors that the company's general manager would apply to the board of directors for a dividend of seven jiao and five fen. Bulls took the opportunity to close out their positions, resulting in a slight decline of around two yuan. In the bond market, foreign bonds were quite strong due to improvements in the European situation, while domestic bonds showed mixed results. The small exchange was weak at the end due to bulls closing out their positions and increased selling. Chicago grains fell due to reports of large wheat imports. The total daily trading volume was 1.28 million shares.

French Divorce Statistics Over the Past Fifty Years 237

—Du

National News Agency dispatch on the tenth: "It has been fifty years since France implemented the divorce law. According to the statistics of the Ministry of Justice, during these fifty years, French courts have approved a total of 722,866 divorces. According to the French divorce law, it was formally promulgated in July 1884 and implemented in September of that year. Within a few months, 1,657 divorce cases were established. By 1885, it had increased to 4,123 cases, and then gradually increased year by year, reaching 28,505 cases in 1931." France is known as a civilized country, and in the past fifty years, its civilization has made rapid progress. The number of divorce cases has also increased day by day. Therefore, I have reached a conclusion that the level of civilization is directly proportional to the number of divorce cases. The higher the level of civilization in a country, the more divorce cases there are.

Our country has always been a country with multiple wives. The higher the official position, the more wives there are. Therefore, being a "king" or "emperor" had the special right to have three wives, nine concubines, twenty-seven concubines, and eighty-one imperial wives. As for later generations, Emperor Taizong of the Tang Dynasty even dismissed as many as 3,000 palace women. Therefore, it was not uncommon for wealthy commoners to have three wives and four concubines. Under this system, there were only "seven outs" provisions, and there was no talk of divorce or no divorce. But what about the average woman? She only had the obligation to respect and abide by the "three obediences and four virtues" and "fidelity until death". Therefore, both parties maintained absolute rights and obligations, and cases of expelling wives were rare, and cases of "being divorced" or "being rejected" were not common. Our country is known as an ancient civilization, but the progress of culture is very slow. Even today, it can only be considered a semi-civilized country, perhaps because there are too few divorce cases.

The period of the fastest cultural advancement in our country is now, and the divorce cases are also like "bamboo shoots after the rain". Because today's marriages are absolutely free for men and women. Freedom to marry means natural freedom to divorce. There is no need to put forward the divorce conditions stipulated in the civil law as a standard. As long as the two parties have some disagreements, or the two parties do not understand each other, they can file for divorce tomorrow. Therefore, in a certain divorce case the other day, on the eve of the hearing, the parties involved "ate at the same table" and "slept in the same bed". The next day in court, the two people "looked at each other and smiled, and were in perfect agreement". Although this type of divorce case is a record-breaking creation, it can be seen that divorce is equal to child's play and is not worth counting. Therefore, the other day there were nine men having sexual relations with a fifteen-year-old girl, but it was just child's play. Try opening the newspaper and taking a look. What day is there no divorce case? Not only are there divorce cases every day, but there are multiple cases in one day. I can see from these divorce cases that our country has truly made civilized progress and that the country is truly promising.

Now, do more divorce suits come from the husband's side? Or do more come from the wife's side? I will not discuss it now. In short, "sons are always your own, wives are always better at other people's homes." This is the common psychology of men. What is the psychology of women? I do not know. I can boldly say that although there are many who are "faithful until death," it cannot be said that there are absolutely none who have the same feelings as men. There used to be an old saying, "Regret three years after your wife dies." It also said, "A farmer who harvests ten more bushels of wheat still wants to change his wife." Because at that time, it was felt that divorce was not easy, so they often dared not do it. They only hoped that their wife would die. The reasons why it was not easy were, first, the constraints of etiquette, and second, the constraints of law. Therefore, they thought about divorce, but never dared to do it. This is probably the reason why the evolution of civilization in our country has stopped.

Therefore, to see the degree of civilized evolution of a country and society, one can look at the number of divorce cases that occur. To take it a step further, to see the degree of personal civilization, one can look at whether the person has divorced or not. Therefore, divorced people are the most civilized and fashionable people. If they hold a "yellow-faced wife" as a treasure, then they are "uncultured" and "unpromising" things. If you observe the degree of civilization in this way, it is probably very accurate, right? Therefore, Western philosophers have said that the more enlightened the people are, the thinner the morals are, which is not bad.

One Hundred Days to Success 238

— Bai Yang

It is said that this year's magazines are popular and called "Magazine Year" because society is progressing, people are becoming more and more busy, and there is no time to match long, huge works. You can only steal a little time to read in the midst of busyness. This reason is quite trustworthy. Hasn't society progressed to the point where a 24-story building has already been completed majestically? And people are becoming more and more busy, even college students are becoming pickpockets. So even bookworms who read day and night are probably going to put down their books and look for a job.

However, in this competitive society, apart

Page 18

from a portion of people who rely on a certain force to hold high positions, most people feel that they do not have enough knowledge and want to read a little more. However, the problem of bread is closely following behind, preventing you from going to college to stroll around like a young master. Therefore, humor and essays are hastily chosen as intellectual food. Although booksellers are worthy of admiration for the hard work of young people, it is like drinking poison to quench thirst, and this morphine needle is not enough to do the job!

Therefore, if you want to seek a cheap, beautiful, and effective entry to learning, then "One Hundred Days to Success" is the answer!

I am one of the 99% of these people, and we should really thank the authors for their kindness, and first shout "One Hundred Days to Success" long live!

After discovering the advertisement, I spent several hours of precious time purchasing "One Hundred Days to Success" from Culture Street. Eagerly reading under the lamp, I spent a week working hard, but the result was nothing. This naturally raises a question: Although "One Hundred Days to Success" is effective quickly, it does not necessarily turn into "Seven Days to Success"? But I think that most of the young people in the group have already been fooled. Alas, long live!

Now, after seeing the "Film Performance One Hundred Days to Success" by Standard Beauty Ms. Xu Lai, I suddenly realized.

Originally, in China, as long as you have appeared on the screen, you are a "star", so there have been quite a few star talents since China had movies. Many non-stars who are eager to choose food want to illegally become "bright," and those rape cases are said to have happened this way, which is not sad! Ms. Xu Lai is called the Standard Beauty, but the image she gives us on the screen is just a "bath". Although the beauty is standard, her screen cultivation is not necessarily a standard star, so this "One Hundred Days to Success" can be imagined, and the rest of the "One Hundred Days to Success" may not be like this!

Impatient friends, how can reading be a hundred days or ten days?

Lonely Mood 239

—Rōnin

Outside the window, the leaves have fallen.

In the distance, the white misty rain obscures the world. Winter rain clouds loom in the sky. The bare branches at the bottom of the fallen leaves in front of the window are struck by the rain, rustling.

It is so lonely, and the mood is so indifferent.

It is winter, the north wind is blowing, thinking of the warm southern country! There are loving mothers, close friends, a warm home, evergreen trees, and beautiful and charming scenery! There, there is no winter, no fallen leaves!

Really tired! So much.

Lazily leaning against the window, looking at the melancholy blue sky, listening to the annoying sound of rain, how deserted the mood feels!

There is no sound of birds, in the cold air, the birds are fleeing! What a cold and lonely atmosphere!

The heart is empty as if there is nothing, and the hands can hardly be lifted. It really feels like a drunk person.

Cherishing the home, cherishing the faint sorrow. The mood is very lonely!

It really feels as lonely as on an island in the Arctic Ocean, as on the deserted island where Robinson lived. But there is still wind howling, and rain dripping.

Looking again at the white misty rain outside the window, and looking at the fallen leaves swirling in the north wind.

"It's the time for the leaves to fall!" That's all I feel, the only feeling I can feel!

What a lonely mood, like being in the desert or on the sea.

Amateur Mailbox

Who is Responsible for Runaway Maids? 240

These are two letters concerning the issue of responsibility in employing servants. Because they are of the same nature, they are published together with some opinions from the editor. It is hoped that readers will discuss them.

(1) Five years ago, a young maid was introduced to me by a relative and employed in my home. Later, because the maid's work was not very satisfactory, I asked the introducer to take her back. However, the introducer insisted that she be kept on due to the girl's poor family situation. Considering humanitarian reasons, I had no choice but to continue employing her. One day, the maid claimed to have something to attend to and wanted to return home. My family allowed her to go. Unexpectedly, the girl never returned. I immediately inquired with the introducer and her family, but they said she never arrived home. I then posted notices everywhere, searching for her, but to no avail. At that time, I convened a meeting with the original introducer, and I paid twenty yuan for overseas travel to compensate for everything, considering it a closed matter. Recently, the family and the introducer have brought up the old matter again, demanding the girl back. I am unable to cope with this. I earnestly request guidance to relieve my worries.

Luo Jiaxiong

(2) A friend of mine purchased a maid through a broker this spring, with a ten-year contract. The maid fell ill in July and died on September 30th.

During her illness, I repeatedly sent letters to the broker and the maid's family, urging them to come and visit. The family replied that they lacked travel funds and therefore could not come. Their letter was sent to a Mr. Jia, a fellow villager, who verbally conveyed this message to my friend's home.

Since the maid became ill, she was taken to the hospital for registration and treatment more than ten times, including two visits to Western doctors (without medical records) and one visit to a Chinese medicine doctor, with a prescription. After the maid died, my friend did not report the death or have an examination performed; instead, he immediately purchased a coffin and prepared for burial. He also sent a letter to the girl's family. Unexpectedly, Mr. Jia, who used to be a lawyer but has been disbarred by the Lawyers Association, instigated the girl's family to accuse my friend of abuse leading to death. The prescription was taken away and hidden by the other party's lawyer under the pretense of investigation.

I have the following two questions and request detailed answers:

(1) If the maid died of illness, but the family was not present at the time of burial, can they accuse him of assault based on this fact?

(2) Is Mr. Jia guilty of instigating the family to falsely accuse my friend of assault?

Li Mengchen

Editor's Note: There are no explicit legal provisions regarding the responsibilities of employers and employees. However, according to general customs, there seems to be a principle that can explain this matter. That is, a servant who is of age and has the capacity for action is difficult, if not impossible, to constantly restrain. Therefore, the employer should not be responsible for any outrageous behavior on their part. The possibility of a servant running away is always present and impossible to prevent. If the employer were always held responsible, who would dare to hire servants? As for younger servants (e.g., fourteen or fifteen years old), the employer's obligation is limited to a certain degree of protection and does not extend to full responsibility.

The editor believes that if a servant is instructed by the employer to do something, such as a very dangerous task, and suffers harm as a result, then the employer should be responsible. Other than that, the employer is not responsible for illness, death, escape, or other such events.

In Luo's case, the young maid ran away without a valid reason. Unless the employer was unreasonably abusive, Luo should not be held absolutely responsible. Even though the maid was young, she would eventually leave the employer. Shopping and going out provided opportunities to escape. How could the employer constantly supervise her? Since the person has already run away, Luo's responsibility is only to assist in the search. Paying money was out of sympathy for the loss of their daughter, but it was a mistake. Perhaps the compensation is the very reason they are seizing the opportunity to extort money. If her family continues to make a fuss and demand the person, then for the sake of future peace, the only solution is to use the law. If money is used to compensate again, we think those people will see that you are easy to bully and will continue to bother you.

Regarding Li's situation, he is certainly not responsible for the death of his maid due to illness. Furthermore, he notified the family in advance and took her to the hospital more than ten times, with consultations from Chinese and Western doctors. This can prove that she died of illness and not from abuse or harm. If Mr. Jia instigated the family to accuse him of abuse leading to death, Li can confront him in court. Although the prescription was taken away, the hospital and Chinese and Western doctors can prove his innocence. When absolutely necessary, an autopsy can be performed to determine if there were any injuries. They are intentionally making false accusations and are therefore guilty. Li's reasons and evidence are sufficient, so it doesn't seem to be a problem.

The contract for buying and selling a maid for a fixed term is not legally valid because a person cannot be bought and sold casually. Although Li's case is in the past, the editor feels it is necessary to inform the general readers.

National Studies 242

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Late Arrival at Ezhou Lu Lun

Clouds clear, seeing Yueyang City in the distance. Still a lonely sail for a day's journey.

The merchant sleeps during the day, knowing the waves are calm. The boatman talks at night, feeling the tide rising.

In the Three Xiang, sad temples meet autumn colors. Ten thousand miles home, facing the bright moon.

Old possessions have been exhausted by war. Even more unbearable is the sound of drums on the river.

Climbing the Liuzhou City Tower, Sending to Zhang Liu Zongyuan

Tingfeng and Lian, Four States Governor

The tall tower on the city connects to the wilderness. Sad thoughts of the sea and sky are vast.

Startling wind ruffles the hibiscus water. Dense rain slants, invading the epiphyte wall.

The mountain trees heavily obscure a thousand miles of sight. The river flow curves like nine intestines.

Together we came to the tattooed land of Baiyue. Still, news is delayed in a single village.

Thinking of Xisai Mountain Liu Yuxi

Wang Jun's warships descended to Yizhou. The royal aura of Jinling was dimmed and subdued.

A thousand fathoms of iron chains sank to the river bottom. A piece of surrender flag came out of the stone.

How many times have past events been grieved in this world? The mountain shape still pillows the cold current.

From now on, the four seas are home. The old graves are bleak in the reeds of autumn.

Shanghai Radio Drama Society

Eternal Life (1080) 4:30 PM to 5:30 PM

"Lonely Wild Duck at Sunset"

Ideals and reality are often contradictory. Just when Feng Yuru wanted to sign an engagement with Jiang Qiuwu, the greedy Mrs. Niu forced her to marry Wang Fucai, who was illiterate. Because Yuru was unwilling to sacrifice her lifelong happiness, she resolutely rejected Niu Tangjian's request. As a result, she could not withstand the coercion and was finally imprisoned in a cold room, enduring the taste of iron bars.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

Facial Damage is Deeply Feared by Actresses 244

— Xi Liu

Rather Lose Life Than Spoil Face - Martha Therefore Died, Carole Dared Not Look in Mirror

No matter how important you say the figure, the limbs, and the hands and feet are in performance, the face is still the most important part for movie stars, especially female stars. They fear that one day their faces will be damaged. Their film life will also be over. They would rather die than have their faces damaged. Therefore, in times of great danger, they will hold their faces with both hands, regardless of their bodies. This is their subconscious action, due to the importance they usually attach to their faces. Years ago, there was a very famous actress, Martha Mansfield. She was on her way home from the photography studio after finishing a film. She was still wearing a costume, made of very thin gauze. After she got into her car, she was exhausted. She struck a match, lit a cigarette, closed her eyes, smoked, and rested very comfortably. Suddenly her clothes caught fire. Martha woke up in shock. She saw the fire and immediately held her face with both hands. The driver immediately stopped the car, ran to the back seat, and shouted, "Quickly put out the fire with your hands!" The fire could have been put out with a single pat, but Martha refused to take her hands away from her face. She was burned all over her body and died, but when she was put in the coffin, her face was still bright and alive. Losing life for the sake of the face is something everyone deeply regrets.

Not many years ago, Carole Lombard's car had an accident and her face was severely injured. She hired several famous surgical experts to sew her face, but they could not guarantee that her face would be restored to its original state. When Carole heard this, the mental pain she suffered could be said to be a hundred times greater than the pain she suffered on her face, because she would rather break like jade than survive like tile. There were many times when she refused to look in the mirror, fearing that she could not bear the pain of a completely broken career. She dared not look at the inevitable reality. After much treatment, the bandages on her face were removed. The doctor told her that her face had miraculously recovered as before, but she still suspected that the doctors were comforting her. She nervously went to get a mirror. When she saw her face, it was indeed undamaged, and she felt that life was meaningful. She now has some fine scars on her face, but some say that the fine scars have increased her beauty, and Carole's reputation has increased tenfold. However, we must understand that Carole Lombard's incident is one in ten million. Apart from that, similar to the above incident was Alice Faye's car accident. She did not damage her face. At that time, she was very grateful that her life was saved, so she did not think about whether her face was damaged or not. But now that she has returned to the photography studio, she thanks God every day for giving her that special favor. She still has a small scar on her left eyelid, which is a souvenir. But that small scar has increased her charm.

Many stars are willing to ride bad horses, drive cars at full speed, play polo, fly planes, hunt, climb mountains, and do all kinds of dangerous games without fear, but when they, or they, have a small pimple on their face, then it's terrible. If an actress breaks her leg, she may only hire one doctor to treat her, but if she breaks a layer of skin on her face, she may hire two doctors, plus a dermatologist. You can't blame them, because their careers depend on their faces. So when Mae West met a robber, the robber pointed a gun at her face and told her to take off her jewelry. Mae calmly said, "Hey, friend, you can take the jewelry, but don't point the gun at my face. You took the jewelry; I can buy it again, but where does the money for another face come from?" Of course, we admire Mae West's courage to dare to talk eloquently in front of the robber, but the robbers knew her psychology, so their second threat was: "If you dare to testify in court and identify me as the person who robbed you, be careful! I will pour nitric acid on your face." Mae West was not afraid, and she still went to court to testify. It wasn't that she didn't value her face, she just refused to be threatened by robbers.

Film Review

Review of "Of Human Bondage" 245

— Shi Fu

Of Human Bondage

— Great Shanghai Screening

The women in this world can only be bought with three things: money, pleasure, and youth. Those who bind themselves with love threads, clinging and sentimental, thinking that they are born to love, are really just big fools who are pitiful and annoying to look at.

The story is about such a big fool: unilaterally loves a fluid woman, everyone thinks "it's not a good marriage," but he himself almost desperately loves her. The first time she married someone else, she was abandoned, and she returned to his arms. The second time she hooked up with his good friend, quarreled with him on purpose, destroyed his beloved famous paintings and books, and made him dizzy with anger. The third time she left him, she only had the road of depravity left.

This fool always has loose strands of connection, never forgetting her. Although there are people who can be gentle and considerate to him, giving him spiritual comfort, they can't resist the enchanting and romantic bad woman. The result of this change is, of course, that the woman ends up in poverty, and the fool finally has the harvest of "heaven does not disappoint those who have a good heart." Finally, he married a virtuous wife.

The script of this play is indeed good, so it is easy for the director to excel, and the impression it gives us is quite profound. What is most enlightening to us is why Leslie Howard has a special fondness for it and must love such a woman who has nothing but "flesh" and is annoying. It can be seen in every place, every era has this kind of "perverted love," which is also the phenomenon of so-called "sea of ​​suffering" and "hell." However, we are "clear observers," so we have this intuition. What we feel here has nothing to do with "love," only "karma." The title "Of Human Bondage" is very correct.

In the photography that tells this story, we see the director's skill. The distribution of roles is not sloppy. In the performance of three different women, the audience is quite satisfied. In addition to Leslie Howard, the two different women manipulators are also well-suited. Whether a play is good or not, we not only look at the protagonist, but I think the emphasis on supporting roles is also more important.

Review of "Wake Up and Dream" 246

— You Jing

Wake up and Dream

In the United States, which is known as the land of gold, even amidst the economic panic and widespread unemployment, the film and song industry appears to be experiencing a distorted prosperity on the surface. However, in reality, female stars and renowned singers also inevitably suffer from the dread of unemployment.

"Wake Up and Dream" vividly portrays the plight of these artists who possess exceptional skills but cannot earn enough to live on.

Kelly is the host of a song and dance troupe, with singers Scotti and female star Toby as the mainstays. However, their business is slow and not enough to make a living. While seeking a way out, they receive a telegram and discover that someone wants to hire another famous singer, Seabro. Kelly falsely claims that Seabro is unwilling to be hired and recommends Scotti and Toby as replacements. Due to Scotti and Toby's artistic talents in the audition, they are finally hired with great difficulty. Unexpectedly, the famous singer suddenly accepts the invitation and arrives. Kelly, posing as a receptionist, gets him drunk and hides him in a secluded room. As a result, the incident is exposed, and they are charged. The three of them have to flee to New York while being pursued by the police.

In the bustling and lively New York, they go to theaters and photography studios of all sizes, but no one is willing to hire them even at the lowest price. They have to work as living advertisements and perform as extras walking on electric wires in extremely tall buildings, risking their lives to earn a small amount of bread.

These descriptions of the suffering of artists in such a society are quite profound. It also touches upon the crime of fraud committed out of necessity for survival, and the misunderstanding of the stage owner who pursues them out of love for their talent, but is mistaken for a police pursuit and is avoided.

Next, Scotti meets his old friend Chilini, a stage tycoon, in a public apartment and returns to Hollywood. Scotti, from being a small cafe employee, is hired by a film company and is able to display his unique skills, becoming famous overnight. Naturally, the story of love is not spared by the producers, and here, the description of the pursuit of life turns into a triangular love affair, culminating in the realization of the dream of fame, fortune, and beauty at the celebratory banquet for their success. In other words, the more meaningful real-life story is sacrificed in a vulgar and decorative conclusion.

Another flaw in the story is the large number of characters involved. Director Kart Neumaph fails to grasp the personalities of the characters, and the overall handling of the film is not very clever. In the first third of the film, the narration of Kelly and others' unemployment, the detention of Seabro, the escape after the incident, and the hardships in New York are concise and clear. The middle part is simply chaotic and ambiguous, leaving the main actors with nothing to do, until later when they are allowed to have a more adequate performance of their love affair.

The main actors, such as Ross Copobu, Laochie Plasi, and Joanne Edward, put in a lot of effort in their performances, but besides the three singing auditions, they did not achieve the success they deserved.

The darker lighting can certainly symbolize a part of their dim lives, but the entire film being like this actually reduces its power.

"Night Blooming Cereus" and "Season of Falling Flowers" Both Begin Filming 247

— Fire

It has been a long time since Cheng Bugao directed "Go to the Northwest" and we haven't seen his new work! All we have seen is that segment he directed in "Daughter's Classic", but it still left a deep impression on countless audiences.

"Night Blooming Cereus" is a script he wrote himself. To make it even better, he spent several sleepless nights carefully writing this work, and it has been successfully filmed in recent days.

The main actors include Hu Die, Zhao Dan, Sun Min, and Shu Xiuwen, who are all praised by the audience as the most talented actors. Of course, under the leadership of director Cheng Bugao, the results will be even more wonderful.

"Season of Falling Flowers" is Wu Cun's new work as a writer and director after "Bigamy". "Bigamy" was an unexpected success, so "Season of Falling Flowers" will go a step further, be more complete, and more watchable.

The main actors include Xu Lai, Gong Jianong, and Zhao Dan, all of whom are veterans of the silver screen. We wish them to bring a different kind of light to the dark film industry. (Que)

A Collection of One Hundred Words 248

— Lin Qin

1.

If foreigners invest in building large film studios in China, I guarantee that China's already fragmented film industry will be even more shattered beyond recognition. A small portion of Chinese practitioners are even willing to be slaves of foreigners, driven by foreigners, to kill China's film industry; how can we not be saddened!

2.

Forget it! If film practitioners don't improve themselves, it is impossible for the general public to value you! You should improve your own private lives, and stop being so shameless in doing those shameless things!

3.

If the editor of a film publication has their own "faction" and their own "preconceived notions," how can we expect to see fair articles?!

4.

"The Goddess" amazed us. It is indeed more practical for a set designer to switch to directing than for a screenwriter to switch to directing!

Film Novel

Interesting Stories of Auctions (I Sell Anything) (III) 249

— Xi Ming

At this time, Groen's palatial residence had become a low-grade antique shop, piled everywhere with furniture, and not even good stuff. Strangely enough, these gentlemen should have suspected Groen's taste, but unfortunately, they always felt that Groen could not be wrong, so they did not investigate. After a while, the auction was about to begin, and everyone was laughing and cheering, as if the Groen family had reached the end of their rope today, and everyone was celebrating. Spod first auctioned off a wooden cabinet. He spoke glibly about the various benefits of the wooden cabinet. As a result, the wooden cabinet sold for three hundred and seventy-five dollars. Spod tried hard to hold back his laughter. He had seen fools on Second Street, and he had seen fools on Old Broadway, but the fools on Fifth Avenue were the most delicious, because the original price of that wooden cabinet was only thirty-five dollars, and the original seller was still waiting for the money. Isn't this interest too good to earn? When Barbara heard the tens, hundreds, and thousands of dollars pouring in like flowing water, she was initially elated, but later she couldn't help but feel scared—what would those wealthy people do after moving the dilapidated furniture into their homes? If an expert pays a little attention to it, then goodbye Spod! As she thought, she counted the checks, all signed by gentlemen, and her hand seemed to be holding a sample book of signatures from a large bank. She looked outward and saw Milison standing next to Spod, listening quietly as Spod eloquently read out each item being auctioned. She couldn't help but shake her head. She knew Milison was no good, just as she knew Milison's golden hair was dyed. She knew Spod was bound to be fooled by Milison. But she felt powerless to help. She couldn't tell him either. Even if she told him, he wouldn't believe it.

Undoubtedly, today's auction was an unexpectedly great success. Just look at those gentlemen and ladies, listening quietly to Spod's big talk, and enjoying it, grabbing to buy without any doubt. After a while, Spod got some free time, jumped to Barbara's side, and instructed her, "Call Monk immediately to the bank and exchange some cash. Tell him to come back right away. Those who supplied the furniture and antiques are still waiting for the money." That's right, those people were still waiting in the next room. They were all Spod's accomplices, all making a living from auctions, but they didn't quite believe it and insisted on waiting for the cash before leaving. Barbara took a roll of checks and handed it to Monk. Monk had already drunk a lot of wine at that time. He took the checks and immediately ran to the bank to exchange them for cash. He took the cash back, but he first needed to find a place to put the cash before handing it over to Spod. He ran upstairs, saw a small wooden box in a small room. He put the large roll of banknotes in the wooden box and locked it. He also locked the small room. Then he found a bed and fell asleep. At this time, Spod had gone mad with the auction, selling everything he saw. He ran to the room where Monk was sleeping, chased away the drowsy Monk, and picked up the furniture to auction it off. He sold the bed, the table, and the chairs. He suddenly saw the small room and wanted to open it, but the door was locked. He couldn't help but be surprised and delighted, "Haha, the door is locked, there must be good stuff inside. I can sell it too." As he spoke, he forcibly broke down the door. He saw a small wooden box inside. He dragged it out. He didn't know that it contained most of the day's income, so he picked it up and auctioned it off. But that box didn't look like a valuable item. No matter how hard you blow your trumpet, the buyers were not enthusiastic. Spod originally wanted to sell it—including the contents—for one hundred dollars. He knew it must be empty, locked by mistake in the furniture store. (To be continued)
